{BhāgPur, 1, 1}
janmādyasya yato 'nvayāditarataś cārtheṣv abhijñaḥ svarāṭ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 1.1]
tene brahma hṛdā ya ādikavaye muhyanti yat sūrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 1.2]
tejovārimṛdāṃ yathā vinimayo yatra trisargo 'mṛṣā | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 1.3]
dhāmnā svena sadā nirastakuhakaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ dhīmahi | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 1.4]
dharmaḥ projjhitakaitavo 'tra paramo nirmatsarāṇāṃ satām | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 2.1]
vedyaṃ vāstavam atra vastu śivadaṃ tāpatrayonmūlanam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 2.2]
śrīmadbhāgavate mahāmunikṛte kiṃ vā parair īśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 2.3]
sadyo hṛdy avarudhyate 'tra kṛtibhiḥ śuśrūṣubhis tatkṣaṇāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 2.4]
nigamakalpatarorgalitaṃ phalam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 3.1]
śukamukhād amṛtadravasaṃyutam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 3.2]
pibata bhāgavataṃ rasam ālayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 3.3]
muhuraho rasikā bhuvi bhāvukāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 3.4]
naimiṣe 'nimiṣakṣetre īśayaḥ śaunakādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 4.1]
sattraṃ svargāya lokāya sahasrasamam āsata | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 4.2]
ta ekadā tu munayaḥ prātarhutahutāgnayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 5.1]
satkṛtaṃ sūtam āsīnaṃ papracchur idam ādarāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 5.2]
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 6.1]
tvayā khalu purāṇāni setihāsāni cānagha | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 6.2]
ākhyātāny apy adhītāni dharmaśāstrāṇi yāny uta | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 6.3]
yāni vedavidāṃ śreṣṭho bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 7.1]
anye ca munayaḥ sūta parāvaravido viduḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 7.2]
vettha tvaṃ saumya tat sarvaṃ tattvatas tadanugrahāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 8.1]
brūyuḥ snigdhasya śiṣyasya guravo guhyam apyuta | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 8.2]
tatra tatrāñjasāyuṣman bhavatā yadviniścitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 9.1]
puṃsām ekāntataḥ śreyastan naḥ śaṃsitum arhasi | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 9.2]
prāyeṇālpāyuṣaḥ sabhya kalāv asmin yuge janāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 10.1]
mandāḥ sumandamatayo mandabhāgyā hy upadrutāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 10.2]
bhūrīṇi bhūrikarmāṇi śrotavyāni vibhāgaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 11.1]
ataḥ sādho 'tra yat sāraṃ samuddhṛtya manīṣayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 11.2]
brūhi bhadrāya bhūtānāṃ yenātmā suprasīdati | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 11.3]
sūta jānāsi bhadraṃ te bhagavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 12.1]
devakyāṃ vasudevasya jāto yasya cikīrṣayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 12.2]
tan naḥ śuśrūṣamāṇānām arhasy aṅgānuvarṇitum | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 13.1]
yasyāvatāro bhūtānāṃ kṣemāya ca bhavāya ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 13.2]
āpannaḥ saṃsṛtiṃ ghorāṃ yan nāma vivaśo gṛṇan | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 14.1]
tataḥ sadyo vimucyeta yadbibheti svayaṃ bhayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 14.2]
yatpādasaṃśrayāḥ sūta munayaḥ praśamāyanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 15.1]
sadyaḥ punanty upaspṛṣṭāḥ svardhunyāpo 'nusevayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 15.2]
ko vā bhagavatastasya puṇyaślokeḍyakarmaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 16.1]
śuddhikāmo na śṛṇuyādyaśaḥ kalimalāpaham | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 16.2]
tasya karmāṇyudārāṇi parigītāni sūribhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 17.1]
brūhi naḥ śraddadhānānāṃ līlayā dadhataḥ kalāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 17.2]
athākhyāhi harerdhīmann avatārakathāḥ śubhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 18.1]
īlā vidadhataḥ svairam īśvarasyātmamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 18.2]
vayaṃ tu na vitṛpyāma uttamaślokavikrame | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 19.1]
yacchṛṇvatāṃ rasajñānāṃ svādu svādu pade pade | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 19.2]
kṛtavān kila karmāṇi saha rāmeṇa keśavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 20.1]
atimartyāni bhagavān gūḍhaḥ kapaṭamānuṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 20.2]
kalim āgatam ājñāya kṣetre 'smin vaiṣṇave vayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 21.1]
āsīnā dīrghasattreṇa kathāyāṃ sakṣaṇā hareḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 21.2]
tvaṃ naḥ saṃdarśito dhātrā dustaraṃ nistitīrṣatām | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 22.1]
kaliṃ sattvaharaṃ puṃsāṃ karṇadhāra ivārṇavam | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 22.2]
brūhi yogeśvare kṛṣṇe brahmaṇye dharmavarmaṇi | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 23.1]
svāṃ kāṣṭhām adhunopete dharmaḥ kaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 1 23.2]
{BhāgPur, 1, 2}
vyāsa uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 1.1]
iti sampraśnasaṃhṛṣṭo viprāṇāṃ raumaharṣaṇiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 1.2]
pratipūjya vacas teṣāṃ pravaktum upacakrame | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 1.3]
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 2.1]
yaṃ pravrajantam anupetam apetakṛtyaṃ dvaipāyano virahakātara ājuhāva | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 2.2]
putreti tanmayatayā taravo 'bhinedus taṃ sarvabhūtahṛdayaṃ munim ānato 'smi | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 2.3]
yaḥ svānubhāvam akhilaśrutisāram ekam adhyātmadīpam atititīrṣatāṃ tamo 'ndham | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 3.1]
saṃsāriṇāṃ karuṇayāha purāṇaguhyaṃ taṃ vyāsasūnum upayāmi guruṃ munīnām | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 3.2]
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 4.1]
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayam udīrayet | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 4.2]
munayaḥ sādhu pṛṣṭo 'haṃ bhavadbhirlokamaṅgalam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 5.1]
yat kṛtaḥ kṛṣṇasampraśno yenātmā suprasīdati | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 5.2]
sa vai puṃsāṃ paro dharmo yato bhaktiradhokṣaje | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 6.1]
ahaitukyapratihatā yayātmā suprasīdati | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 6.2]
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ prayojitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 7.1]
janayatyāśu vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ ca yadahaitukam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 7.2]
dharmaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ puṃsāṃ viṣvaksenakathāsu yaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 8.1]
notpādayedyadi ratiṃ śrama eva hi kevalam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 8.2]
dharmasya hy āpavargyasya nārtho 'rthāyopakalpate | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 9.1]
nārthasya dharmaikāntasya kāmo lābhāya hi smṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 9.2]
kāmasya nendriyaprītirlābho jīveta yāvatā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 10.1]
jīvasya tattvajijñāsā nārtho yaśceha karmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 10.2]
vadanti tat tattvavidastattvaṃ yaj jñānam advayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 11.1]
brahmeti paramātmeti bhagavān iti śabdyate | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 11.2]
tacchraddadhānā munayo jñānavairāgyayuktayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 12.1]
paśyantyātmani cātmānaṃ bhaktyā śrutagṛhītayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 12.2]
ataḥ puṃbhir dvijaśreṣṭhā varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 13.1]
svanuṣṭhitasya dharmasya saṃsiddhirharitoṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 13.2]
tasmādekena manasā bhagavān sātvatāṃ patiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 14.1]
śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaś ca dhyeyaḥ pūjyaśca nityadā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 14.2]
yad anudhyāsinā yuktāḥ karmagranthinibandhanam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 15.1]
chindanti kovidāstasya ko na kuryāt kathāratim | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 15.2]
śuśrūṣoḥ śraddadhānasya vāsudevakathāruciḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 16.1]
syān mahatsevayā viprāḥ puṇyatīrthaniṣevaṇāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 16.2]
śṛṇvatāṃ svakathāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 17.1]
hṛdyantaḥstho hy abhadrāṇi vidhunoti suhṛtsatām | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 17.2]
naṣṭaprāyeṣvabhadreṣu nityaṃ bhāgavatasevayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 18.1]
bhagavatyuttamaśloke bhaktirbhavati naiṣṭhikī | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 18.2]
tadā rajastamobhāvāḥ kāmalobhādayaśca ye | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 19.1]
ceta etair anāviddhaṃ sthitaṃ sattve prasīdati | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 19.2]
evaṃ prasannamanaso bhagavadbhaktiyogataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 20.1]
bhagavattattvavijñānaṃ muktasaṅgasya jāyate | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 20.2]
bhidyate hṛdayagranthiśchidyante sarvasaṃśayāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 21.1]
kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi dṛṣṭa evātmanīśvare | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 21.2]
ato vai kavayo nityaṃ bhaktiṃ paramayā mudā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 22.1]
vāsudeve bhagavati kurvantyātmaprasādanīm | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 22.2]
sattvaṃ rajastama iti prakṛterguṇāstair yuktaḥ paramapuruṣa eka ihāsya dhatte | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 23.1]
sthityādaye hariviriñcihareti saṃjñāḥ śreyāṃsi tatra khalu sattvatanor nṝṇāṃ syuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 23.2]
pārthivād dāruṇo dhūmas tasmād agnistrayīmayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 24.1]
tamasastu rajastasmāt sattvaṃ yadbrahmadarśanam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 24.2]
bhejire munayo 'thāgre bhagavantam adhokṣajam | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 25.1]
sattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ kṣemāya kalpante ye 'nu tān iha | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 25.2]
mumukṣavo ghorarūpān hitvā bhūtapatīn atha | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 26.1]
nārāyaṇakalāḥ śāntā bhajanti hy anasūyavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 26.2]
rajastamaḥprakṛtayaḥ samaśīlā bhajanti vai | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 27.1]
pitṛbhūtaprajeśādīn śriyaiśvaryaprajepsavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 27.2]
vāsudevaparā vedā vāsudevaparā makhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 28.1]
vāsudevaparā yogo vāsudevaparāḥ kriyāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 28.2]
vāsudevaparaṃ jñānaṃ vāsudevaparaṃ tapaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 29.1]
vāsudevaparo dharmo vāsudevaparā gatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 29.2]
sa evedaṃ sasarjāgre bhagavān ātmamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 30.1]
sadasadrūpayā cāsau guṇamayāguṇo vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 30.2]
tayā vilasiteṣv eṣu guṇeṣu guṇavān iva | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 31.1]
antaḥpraviṣṭa ābhāti vijñānena vijṛmbhitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 31.2]
yathā hy avahito vahnirdāruṣvekaḥ svayoniṣu | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 32.1]
nāneva bhāti viśvātmā bhūteṣu ca tathā pumān | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 32.2]
asau guṇamayair bhāvair bhūtasūkṣmendriyātmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 33.1]
svanirmiteṣu nirviṣṭo bhuṅkte bhūteṣu tadguṇān | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 33.2]
bhāvayaty eṣa sattvena lokān vai lokabhāvanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 34.1]
līlāvatārānurato devatiryaṅnarādiṣu | [BhāgPur, 1, 2 34.2]
{BhāgPur, 1, 3}
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 1.1]
jagṛhe pauruṣaṃ rūpaṃ bhagavān mahadādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 1.2]
sambhūtaṃ ṣoḍaśakalam ādau lokasisṛkṣayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 2.1]
yasyāmbhasi śayānasya yoganidrāṃ vitanvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 2.2]
nābhihradāmbujādāsīdbrahmā viśvasṛjāṃ patiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 3.1]
yasyāvayavasaṃsthānaiḥ kalpito lokavistaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 3.2]
tadvai bhagavato rūpaṃ viśuddhaṃ sattvam ūrjitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 4.1]
paśyantyado rūpam adabhracakṣuṣā sahasrapādorubhujānanādbhutam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 4.2]
sahasramūrdhaśravaṇākṣināsikaṃ sahasramaulyambarakuṇḍalollasat | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 5.1]
etan nānāvatārāṇāṃ nidhānaṃ bījam avyayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 5.2]
yasyāṃśāṃśena sṛjyante devatiryaṅnarādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 6.1]
sa eva prathamaṃ devaḥ kaumāraṃ sargam āśritaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 6.2]
cacāra duścaraṃ brahmā brahmacaryam akhaṇḍitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 7.1]
dvitīyaṃ tu bhavāyāsya rasātalagatāṃ mahīm | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 7.2]
uddhariṣyann upādatta yajñeśaḥ saukaraṃ vapuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 8.1]
tṛtīyam ṛṣisargaṃ vai devarṣitvam upetya saḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 8.2]
tantraṃ sātvatam ācaṣṭa naiṣkarmyaṃ karmaṇāṃ yataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 9.1]
turye dharmakalāsarge naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 9.2]
bhūtvātmopaśamopetam akarod duścaraṃ tapaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 10.1]
pañcamaḥ kapilo nāma siddheśaḥ kālaviplutam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 10.2]
provācāsuraye sāṃkhyaṃ tattvagrāmavinirṇayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 11.1]
ṣaṣṭham atrerapatyatvaṃ vṛtaḥ prāpto 'nasūyayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 11.2]
ānvīkṣikīm alarkāya prahlādādibhya ūcivān | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 12.1]
tataḥ saptama ākūtyāṃ ruceryajño 'bhyajāyata | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 12.2]
sa yāmādyaiḥ suragaṇairapāt svāyambhuvāntaram | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 13.1]
aṣṭame merudevyāṃ tu nābherjāta urukramaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 13.2]
darśayan vartma dhīrāṇāṃ sarvāśramanamaskṛtam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 14.1]
ṛṣibhiryācito bheje navamaṃ pārthivaṃ vapuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 14.2]
dugdhemām oṣadhīr viprās tenāyaṃ sa uśattamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 15.1]
rūpaṃ sa jagṛhe mātsyaṃ cākṣuṣodadhisamplave | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 15.2]
nāvyāropya mahīmayyām apādvaivasvataṃ manum | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 16.1]
surāsurāṇām udadhiṃ mathnatāṃ mandarācalam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 16.2]
dadhre kamaṭharūpeṇa pṛṣṭha ekādaśe vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 17.1]
dhānvantaraṃ dvādaśamaṃ trayodaśamam eva ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 17.2]
apāyayat surān anyān mohinyā mohayan striyā | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 18.1]
caturdaśaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ bibhrad daityendram ūrjitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 18.2]
dadāra karajair ūrāv erakāṃ kaṭakṛdyathā | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 19.1]
pañcadaśaṃ vāmanakaṃ kṛtvāgādadhvaraṃ baleḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 19.2]
padatrayaṃ yācamānaḥ pratyāditsus tripiṣṭapam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 20.1]
avatāre ṣoḍaśame paśyan brahmadruho nṛpān | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 20.2]
triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ kupito niḥkṣatrām akaron mahīm | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 21.1]
tataḥ saptadaśe jātaḥ satyavatyāṃ parāśarāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 21.2]
cakre vedataroḥ śākhā dṛṣṭvā puṃso 'lpamedhasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 22.1]
naradevatvam āpannaḥ surakāryacikīrṣayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 22.2]
samudranigrahādīni cakre vīryāṇyataḥ param | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 23.1]
ekonaviṃśe viṃśatime vṛṣṇiṣu prāpya janmanī | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 23.2]
rāmakṛṣṇāv iti bhuvo bhagavān aharadbharam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 24.1]
tataḥ kalau sampravṛtte sammohāya suradviṣām | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 24.2]
buddho nāmnāñjanasutaḥ kīkaṭeṣu bhaviṣyati | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 25.1]
athāsau yugasaṃdhyāyāṃ dasyuprāyeṣu rājasu | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 25.2]
janitā viṣṇuyaśaso nāmnā kalkirjagatpatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 26.1]
avatārā hy asaṃkhyeyā hareḥ sattvanidherdvijāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 26.2]
yathāvidāsinaḥ kulyāḥ sarasaḥ syuḥ sahasraśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 27.1]
ṛṣayo manavo devā manuputrā mahaujasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 27.2]
kalāḥ sarve harereva saprajāpatayaḥ smṛtāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 28.1]
ete cāṃśakalāḥ puṃsaḥ kṛṣṇastu bhagavān svayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 28.2]
indrārivyākulaṃ lokaṃ mṛḍayanti yuge yuge | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 29.1]
janma guhyaṃ bhagavato ya etat prayato naraḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 29.2]
sāyaṃ prātargṛṇan bhaktyā duḥkhagrāmādvimucyate | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 30.1]
etadrūpaṃ bhagavato hy arūpasya cidātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 30.2]
māyāguṇair viracitaṃ mahadādibhirātmani | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 31.1]
yathā nabhasi meghaugho reṇurvā pārthivo 'nile | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 31.2]

evaṃ ca janmāni karmāṇi hy akartur ajanasya ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 35.2]
varṇayanti sma kavayo vedaguhyāni hṛtpateḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 36.1]
sa vā idaṃ viśvam amoghalīlaḥ sṛjaty avaty atti na sajjate 'smin | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 36.2]

na cāsya kaścin nipuṇena dhātur avaiti jantuḥ kumanīṣa ūtīḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 37.2]

sa veda dhātuḥ padavīṃ parasya durantavīryasya rathāṅgapāṇeḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 38.2]
yo 'māyayā saṃtatayānuvṛttyā bhajeta tatpādasarojagandham | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 39.1]

idaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma purāṇaṃ brahmasaṃmitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 40.2]
uttamaślokacaritaṃ cakāra bhagavān ṛṣiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 41.1]
niḥśreyasāya lokasya dhanyaṃ svastyayanaṃ mahat | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 41.2]
tadidaṃ grāhayāmāsa sutam ātmavatāṃ varam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 42.1]
sarvavedetihāsānāṃ sāraṃ sāraṃ samuddhṛtam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 42.2]
sa tu saṃśrāvayāmāsa mahārājaṃ parīkṣitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 43.1]
prāyopaviṣṭaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ parītaṃ paramarṣibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 43.2]
kṛṣṇe svadhāmopagate dharmajñānādibhiḥ saha | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 44.1]
kalau naṣṭadṛśām eṣa purāṇārko 'dhunoditaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 3 44.2]

{BhāgPur, 1, 4}

kathaṃ sa vīraḥ śriyam aṅga dustyajāṃ yuvaiṣatotsraṣṭum aho sahāsubhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 11.2]
śivāya lokasya bhavāya bhūtaye ya uttamaślokaparāyaṇā janāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 12.1]
jīvanti nātmārtham asau parāśrayaṃ mumoca nirvidya kutaḥ kalevaram | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 12.2]
tat sarvaṃ naḥ samācakṣva pṛṣṭo yadiha kiṃcana | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 13.1]
manye tvāṃ viṣaye vācāṃ snātam anyatra chāndasāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 13.2]
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 14.1]
dvāpare samanuprāpte tṛtīye yugaparyaye | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 14.2]
jātaḥ parāśarādyogī vāsavyāṃ kalayā hareḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 14.3]
sa kadācit sarasvatyā upaspṛśya jalaṃ śuciḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 15.1]

itihāsapurāṇānāṃ pitā me romaharṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 22.2]

iti bhāratam ākhyānaṃ kṛpayā muninā kṛtam | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 25.3]
evaṃ pravṛttasya sadā bhūtānāṃ śreyasi dvijāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 26.1]
sarvātmakenāpi yadā nātuṣyaddhṛdayaṃ tataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 26.2]

dhṛtavratena hi mayā chandāṃsi guravo 'gnayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 28.1]

tathāpi bata me daihyo hy ātmā caivātmanā vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 30.1]
asaṃpanna ivābhāti brahmavarcasya sattamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 4 30.2]

{BhāgPur, 1, 5}
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 1.1]
atha taṃ sukham āsīna upāsīnaṃ bṛhacchravāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 1.2]
devarṣiḥ prāha viprarṣiṃ vīṇāpāṇiḥ smayann iva | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 1.3]
nārada uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 2.1]
pārāśarya mahābhāga bhavataḥ kaccid ātmanā | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 2.2]
parituṣyati śārīra ātmā mānasa eva vā | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 2.3]
jijñāsitaṃ susampannam api te mahadadbhutam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 3.1]

sa vai bhavān veda samastaguhyam upāsito yat puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 6.1]
parāvareśo manasaiva viśvaṃ sṛjatyavatyatti guṇairasaṅgaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 6.2]

śrīnārada uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 8.1]
bhavatānuditaprāyaṃ yaśo bhagavato 'malam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 8.2]
yenaivāsau na tuṣyeta manye taddarśanaṃ khilam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 8.3]
yathā dharmādayaścārthā munivaryānukīrtitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 9.1]
na tathā vāsudevasya mahimā hy anuvarṇitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 9.2]
na yad vacaś citrapadaṃ hareryaśo jagatpavitraṃ pragṛṇīta karhicit | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 10.1]

tadvāgvisargo janatāghaviplavo yasmin pratiślokam abaddhavatyapi | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 11.1]
nāmānyanantasya yaśo 'ṅkitāni yat śṛṇvanti gāyanti gṛṇanti sādhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 11.2]
naiṣkarmyam apyacyutabhāvavarjitaṃ na śobhate jñānam alaṃ nirañjanam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 12.1]
kutaḥ punaḥ śaśvadabhadram īśvare na cārpitaṃ karma yadapyakāraṇam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 12.2]
atho mahābhāga bhavān amoghadṛk śuciśravāḥ satyarato dhṛtavrataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 13.1]
urukramasyākhilabandhamuktaye samādhinānusmara tadviceṣṭitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 13.2]
tato 'nyathā kiṃcana yadvivakṣataḥ pṛthag dṛśastatkṛtarūpanāmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 14.1]
na karhicit kvāpi ca duḥsthitā matir labheta vātāhatanaurivāspadam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 14.2]
jugupsitaṃ dharmakṛte 'nuśāsataḥ svabhāvaraktasya mahān vyatikramaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 15.1]
yadvākyato dharma itītaraḥ sthito na manyate tasya nivāraṇaṃ janaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 15.2]
vicakṣaṇo 'syārhati vedituṃ vibhor anantapārasya nivṛttitaḥ sukham | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 16.1]

yatra kva vābhadram abhūdamuṣya kiṃ ko vārtha āpto 'bhajatāṃ svadharmataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 17.2]
tasyaiva hetoḥ prayateta kovido na labhyate yadbhramatām uparyadhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 18.1]

idaṃ hi viśvaṃ bhagavān ivetaro yato jagatsthānanirodhasambhavāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 20.1]

ucchiṣṭalepān anumodito dvijaiḥ sakṛt sma bhuñje tadapāstakilbiṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 25.1]
evaṃ pravṛttasya viśuddhacetasas taddharma evātmaruciḥ prajāyate | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 25.2]
tatrānvahaṃ kṛṣṇakathāḥ pragāyatām anugraheṇāśṛṇavaṃ manoharāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 26.1]
tāḥ śraddhayā me 'nupadaṃ viśṛṇvataḥ priyaśravasyaṅga mamābhavadruciḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 26.2]
tasmiṃstadā labdharucermahāmate priyaśravasyaskhalitā matirmama | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 27.1]
yayāham etat sadasat svamāyayā paśye mayi brahmaṇi kalpitaṃ pare | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 27.2]
itthaṃ śaratprāvṛṣikāv ṛtū harer viśṛṇvato me 'nusavaṃ yaśo 'malam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 28.1]
saṃkīrtyamānaṃ munibhirmahātmabhir bhaktiḥ pravṛttātmarajastamo'pahā | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 28.2]
tasyaivaṃ me 'nuraktasya praśritasya hatainasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 29.1]
śraddadhānasya bālasya dāntasyānucarasya ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 29.2]
jñānaṃ guhyatamaṃ yat tat sākṣādbhagavatoditam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 30.1]
anvavocan gamiṣyantaḥ kṛpayā dīnavatsalāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 30.2]
yenaivāhaṃ bhagavato vāsudevasya vedhasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 31.1]

etat saṃsūcitaṃ brahmaṃstāpatrayacikitsitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 32.1]
yadīśvare bhagavati karma brahmaṇi bhāvitam | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 32.2]

kurvāṇā yatra karmāṇi bhagavacchikṣayāsakṛt | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 36.1]
gṛṇanti guṇanāmāni kṛṣṇasyānusmaranti ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 36.2]
oṃ namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ vāsudevāya dhīmahi | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 37.1]
pradyumnāyāniruddhāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 5 37.2]

sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 1.1]
yo vai drauṇyastravipluṣṭo na māturudare mṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 1.2]

upavarṇitam etadvaḥ puṇyaṃ pārīkṣitaṃ mayā | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 9.1]

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 11.1]
sūta jīva samāḥ saumya śāśvatīrviśadaṃ yaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 11.2]
yastvaṃ śaṃsasi kṛṣṇasya martyānām amṛtaṃ hi naḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 11.3]
karmaṇyasminn anāśvāse dhūmadhūmrātmanāṃ bhavān | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 12.1]
āpāyayati govinda pādapadmāsavaṃ madhu | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 12.2]
tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 13.1]
bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 13.2]
ko nāma tṛpyedrasavit kathāyāṃ mahattamaikāntaparāyaṇasya | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 14.1]
nāntaṃ guṇānām aguṇasya jagmur yogeśvarā ye bhavapādmamukhyāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 14.2]
tan no bhavān vai bhagavatpradhāno mahattamaikāntaparāyaṇasya | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 15.1]
harerudāraṃ caritaṃ viśuddhaṃ śuśrūṣatāṃ no vitanotu vidvan | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 15.2]
sa vai mahābhāgavataḥ parīkṣid yenāpavargākhyam adabhrabuddhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 16.1]

sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 18.1]

ekadā dhanurudyamya vicaran mṛgayāṃ vane | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 24.1]

pratiruddhendriyaprāṇamanobuddhim upāratam | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 26.1]
sthānatrayāt paraṃ prāptaṃ brahmabhūtam avikriyam | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 26.2]
viprakīrṇajaṭācchannaṃ rauraveṇājinena ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 27.1]
viśuṣyattālurudakaṃ tathābhūtam ayācata | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 27.2]
alabdhatṛṇabhūmyādir asaṃprāptārghyasūnṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 28.1]
avajñātam ivātmānaṃ manyamānaścukopa ha | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 28.2]
abhūtapūrvaḥ sahasā kṣuttṛḍbhyām arditātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 29.1]
brāhmaṇaṃ pratyabhūdbrahman matsaro manyureva ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 29.2]
sa tu brahmaṛṣeraṃse gatāsum uragaṃ ruṣā | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 30.1]
vinirgacchan dhanuṣkoṭyā nidhāya puram āgataḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 30.2]
eṣa kiṃ nibhṛtāśeṣakaraṇo mīlitekṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 31.1]

tasya putro 'titejasvī viharan bālako 'rbhakaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 32.1]
rājñāghaṃ prāpitaṃ tātaṃ śrutvā tatredam abravīt | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 32.2]

kena vā te 'pakṛtam ityuktaḥ sa nyavedayat | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 40.2]
niśamya śaptam atadarhaṃ narendraṃ sa brāhmaṇo nātmajam abhyanandat | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 41.1]
aho batāṃho mahadadya te kṛtam alpīyasi droha ururdamo dhṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 18 41.2]

{BhāgPur, 1, 19}
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 1.1]
mahīpatistvatha tatkarma garhyaṃ vicintayann ātmakṛtaṃ sudurmanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 1.2]
aho mayā nīcam anāryavat kṛtaṃ nirāgasi brahmaṇi gūḍhatejasi | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 1.3]
dhruvaṃ tato me kṛtadevahelanād duratyayaṃ vyasanaṃ nātidīrghāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 2.1]
tadastu kāmaṃ hyaghaniṣkṛtāya me yathā na kuryāṃ punarevam addhā | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 2.2]
adyaiva rājyaṃ balam ṛddhakośaṃ prakopitabrahmakulānalo me | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 3.1]
dahatvabhadrasya punarna me 'bhūt pāpīyasī dhīrdvijadevagobhyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 3.2]
sa cintayann ittham athāśṛṇodyathā muneḥ sutokto nirṛtistakṣakākhyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 4.1]
sa sādhu mene na cireṇa takṣakā nalaṃ prasaktasya viraktikāraṇam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 4.2]
atho vihāyemam amuṃ ca lokaṃ vimarśitau heyatayā purastāt | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 5.1]
kṛṣṇāṅghrisevām adhimanyamāna upāviśat prāyam amartyanadyām | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 5.2]
yā vai lasacchrītulasīvimiśrakṛṣṇāṅghrireṇvabhyadhikāmbunetrī | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 6.1]
punāti lokān ubhayatra seśān kastāṃ na seveta mariṣyamāṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 6.2]
iti vyavacchidya sa pāṇḍaveyaḥ prāyopaveśaṃ prati viṣṇupadyām | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 7.1]
dadhau mukundāṅghrim ananyabhāvo munivrato muktasamastasaṅgaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 7.2]
tatropajagmurbhuvanaṃ punānā mahānubhāvā munayaḥ saśiṣyāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 8.1]
prāyeṇa tīrthābhigamāpadeśaiḥ svayaṃ hi tīrthāni punanti santaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 8.2]
atrirvasiṣṭhaścyavanaḥ śaradvān ariṣṭanemirbhṛguraṅgirāśca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 9.1]
parāśaro gādhisuto 'tha rāma utathya indrapramadedhmavāhau | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 9.2]
medhātithirdevala ārṣṭiṣeṇo bhāradvājo gautamaḥ pippalādaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 10.1]
maitreya aurvaḥ kavaṣaḥ kumbhayonir dvaipāyano bhagavān nāradaśca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 10.2]
anye ca devarṣibrahmarṣivaryā rājarṣivaryā aruṇādayaśca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 11.1]
nānārṣeyapravarān sametān abhyarcya rājā śirasā vavande | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 11.2]
sukhopaviṣṭeṣvatha teṣu bhūyaḥ kṛtapraṇāmaḥ svacikīrṣitaṃ yat | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 12.1]
vijñāpayāmāsa viviktacetā upasthito 'gre 'bhigṛhītapāṇiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 12.2]
rājovāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 13.1]
aho vayaṃ dhanyatamā nṛpāṇāṃ mahattamānugrahaṇīyaśīlāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 13.2]
rājñāṃ kulaṃ brāhmaṇapādaśaucād dūrādvisṛṣṭaṃ bata garhyakarma | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 13.3]
tasyaiva me 'ghasya parāvareśo vyāsaktacittasya gṛheṣvabhīkṣṇam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 14.1]
nirvedamūlo dvijaśāparūpo yatra prasakto bhayam āśu dhatte | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 14.2]
taṃ mopayātaṃ pratiyantu viprā gaṅgā ca devī dhṛtacittam īśe | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 15.1]
dvijopasṛṣṭaḥ kuhakastakṣako vā daśatvalaṃ gāyata viṣṇugāthāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 15.2]
punaśca bhūyādbhagavatyanante ratiḥ prasaṅgaśca tadāśrayeṣu | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 16.1]
mahatsu yāṃ yām upayāmi sṛṣṭiṃ maitryastu sarvatra namo dvijebhyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 16.2]
iti sma rājādhyavasāyayuktaḥ prācīnamūleṣu kuśeṣu dhīraḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 17.1]
udaṅmukho dakṣiṇakūla āste samudrapatnyāḥ svasutanyastabhāraḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 17.2]
evaṃ ca tasmin naradevadeve prāyopaviṣṭe divi devasaṅghāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 18.1]
praśasya bhūmau vyakiran prasūnair mudā muhurdundubhayaśca neduḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 18.2]
maharṣayo vai samupāgatā ye praśasya sādhvityanumodamānāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 19.1]
ūcuḥ prajānugrahaśīlasārā yaduttamaślokaguṇābhirūpam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 19.2]
na vā idaṃ rājarṣivarya citraṃ bhavatsu kṛṣṇaṃ samanuvrateṣu | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 20.1]
ye 'dhyāsanaṃ rājakirīṭajuṣṭaṃ sadyo jahurbhagavatpārśvakāmāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 20.2]
sarve vayaṃ tāvadihāsmahe 'tha kalevaraṃ yāvadasau vihāya | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 21.1]
lokaṃ paraṃ virajaskaṃ viśokaṃ yāsyatyayaṃ bhāgavatapradhānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 21.2]
āśrutya tadṛṣigaṇavacaḥ parīkṣit samaṃ madhucyudguru cāvyalīkam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 22.1]
ābhāṣatainān abhinandya yuktān śuśrūṣamāṇaścaritāni viṣṇoḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 22.2]
samāgatāḥ sarvata eva sarve vedā yathā mūrtidharāstripṛṣṭhe | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 23.1]
nehātha nāmutra ca kaścanārtha ṛte parānugraham ātmaśīlam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 23.2]
tataśca vaḥ pṛcchyam imaṃ vipṛcche viśrabhya viprā iti kṛtyatāyām | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 24.1]
sarvātmanā mriyamāṇaiśca kṛtyaṃ śuddhaṃ ca tatrāmṛśatābhiyuktāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 24.2]
tatrābhavadbhagavān vyāsaputro yadṛcchayā gām aṭamāno 'napekṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 25.1]
alakṣyaliṅgo nijalābhatuṣṭo vṛtaśca bālairavadhūtaveṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 25.2]
taṃ dvyaṣṭavarṣaṃ sukumārapādakarorubāhvaṃsakapolagātram | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 26.1]
cārvāyatākṣonnasatulyakarṇasubhrvānanaṃ kambusujātakaṇṭham | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 26.2]
nigūḍhajatruṃ pṛthutuṅgavakṣasam āvartanābhiṃ valivalgūdaraṃ ca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 27.1]
digambaraṃ vaktravikīrṇakeśaṃ pralambabāhuṃ svamarottamābham | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 27.2]
śyāmaṃ sadāpīvyavayo'ṅgalakṣmyā strīṇāṃ manojñaṃ rucirasmitena | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 28.1]
pratyutthitāste munayaḥ svāsanebhyas tallakṣaṇajñā api gūḍhavarcasam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 28.2]
sa viṣṇurāto 'tithaya āgatāya tasmai saparyāṃ śirasājahāra | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 29.1]
tato nivṛttā hyabudhāḥ striyo 'rbhakā mahāsane sopaviveśa pūjitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 29.2]
sa saṃvṛtastatra mahān mahīyasāṃ brahmarṣirājarṣidevarṣisaṅghaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 30.1]
vyarocatālaṃ bhagavān yathendur graharkṣatārānikaraiḥ parītaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 30.2]
praśāntam āsīnam akuṇṭhamedhasaṃ muniṃ nṛpo bhāgavato 'bhyupetya | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 31.1]
praṇamya mūrdhnāvahitaḥ kṛtāñjalir natvā girā sūnṛtayānvapṛcchat | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 31.2]
parīkṣiduvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 32.1]
aho adya vayaṃ brahman satsevyāḥ kṣatrabandhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 32.2]
kṛpayātithirūpeṇa bhavadbhistīrthakāḥ kṛtāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 32.3]
yeṣāṃ saṃsmaraṇāt puṃsāṃ sadyaḥ śudhyanti vai gṛhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 33.1]
kiṃ punardarśanasparśapādaśaucāsanādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 33.2]
sānnidhyāt te mahāyogin pātakāni mahāntyapi | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 34.1]
sadyo naśyanti vai puṃsāṃ viṣṇoriva suretarāḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 34.2]
api me bhagavān prītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍusutapriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 35.1]
paitṛṣvaseyaprītyarthaṃ tadgotrasyāttabāndhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 35.2]
anyathā te 'vyaktagaterdarśanaṃ naḥ kathaṃ nṛṇām | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 36.1]
nitarāṃ mriyamāṇānāṃ saṃsiddhasya vanīyasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 36.2]
ataḥ pṛcchāmi saṃsiddhiṃ yogināṃ paramaṃ gurum | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 37.1]
puruṣasyeha yat kāryaṃ mriyamāṇasya sarvathā | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 37.2]
yacchrotavyam atho japyaṃ yat kartavyaṃ nṛbhiḥ prabho | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 38.1]
smartavyaṃ bhajanīyaṃ vā brūhi yadvā viparyayam | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 38.2]
nūnaṃ bhagavato brahman gṛheṣu gṛhamedhinām | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 39.1]
na lakṣyate hyavasthānam api godohanaṃ kvacit | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 39.2]
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 40.1]
evam ābhāṣitaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sa rājñā ślakṣṇayā girā | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 40.2]
pratyabhāṣata dharmajño bhagavān bādarāyaṇiḥ | [BhāgPur, 1, 19 40.3]
{BhāgPur, 2, 1}
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 1.1]
varīyān eṣa te praśnaḥ kṛto lokahitaṃ nṛpa | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 1.2]
ātmavitsaṃmataḥ puṃsāṃ śrotavyādiṣu yaḥ paraḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 1.3]
śrotavyādīni rājendra nṛṇāṃ santi sahasraśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 2.1]
apaśyatām ātmatattvaṃ gṛheṣu gṛhamedhinām | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 2.2]
nidrayā hriyate naktaṃ vyavāyena ca vā vayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 3.1]
divā cārthehayā rājan kuṭumbabharaṇena vā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 3.2]
dehāpatyakalatrādiṣvātmasainyeṣvasatsvapi | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 4.1]
teṣāṃ pramatto nidhanaṃ paśyann api na paśyati | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 4.2]
tasmādbhārata sarvātmā bhagavān īśvaro hariḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 5.1]
śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaśca smartavyaścecchatābhayam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 5.2]
etāvān sāṅkhyayogābhyāṃ svadharmapariniṣṭhayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 6.1]
janmalābhaḥ paraḥ puṃsām ante nārāyaṇasmṛtiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 6.2]
prāyeṇa munayo rājan nivṛttā vidhiṣedhataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 7.1]
nairguṇyasthā ramante sma guṇānukathane hareḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 7.2]
idaṃ bhāgavataṃ nāma purāṇaṃ brahmasaṃmitam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 8.1]
adhītavān dvāparādau piturdvaipāyanādaham | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 8.2]
pariniṣṭhito 'pi nairguṇya uttamaślokalīlayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 9.1]
gṛhītacetā rājarṣe ākhyānaṃ yadadhītavān | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 9.2]
tadahaṃ te 'bhidhāsyāmi mahāpauruṣiko bhavān | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 10.1]
yasya śraddadhatām āśu syān mukunde matiḥ satī | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 10.2]
etan nirvidyamānānām icchatām akutobhayam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 11.1]
yogināṃ nṛpa nirṇītaṃ harernāmānukīrtanam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 11.2]
kiṃ pramattasya bahubhiḥ parokṣairhāyanairiha | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 12.1]
varaṃ muhūrtaṃ viditaṃ ghaṭate śreyase yataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 12.2]
khaṭvāṅgo nāma rājarṣirjñātveyattām ihāyuṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 13.1]
muhūrtāt sarvam utsṛjya gatavān abhayaṃ harim | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 13.2]
tavāpyetarhi kauravya saptāhaṃ jīvitāvadhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 14.1]
upakalpaya tat sarvaṃ tāvadyat sāmparāyikam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 14.2]
antakāle tu puruṣa āgate gatasādhvasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 15.1]
chindyādasaṅgaśastreṇa spṛhāṃ dehe 'nu ye ca tam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 15.2]
gṛhāt pravrajito dhīraḥ puṇyatīrthajalāplutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 16.1]
śucau vivikta āsīno vidhivat kalpitāsane | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 16.2]
abhyasen manasā śuddhaṃ trivṛdbrahmākṣaraṃ param | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 17.1]
mano yacchejjitaśvāso brahmabījam avismaran | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 17.2]
niyacchedviṣayebhyo 'kṣān manasā buddhisārathiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 18.1]
manaḥ karmabhirākṣiptaṃ śubhārthe dhārayeddhiyā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 18.2]
tatraikāvayavaṃ dhyāyedavyucchinnena cetasā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 19.1]
mano nirviṣayaṃ yuktvā tataḥ kiṃcana na smaret | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 19.2]
padaṃ tat paramaṃ viṣṇormano yatra prasīdati | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 19.3]
rajastamobhyām ākṣiptaṃ vimūḍhaṃ mana ātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 20.1]
yaccheddhāraṇayā dhīro hanti yā tatkṛtaṃ malam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 20.2]
yasyāṃ saṃdhāryamāṇāyāṃ yogino bhaktilakṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 21.1]
āśu sampadyate yoga āśrayaṃ bhadram īkṣataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 21.2]
rājovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 22.1]
yathā saṃdhāryate brahman dhāraṇā yatra saṃmatā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 22.2]
yādṛśī vā haredāśu puruṣasya manomalam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 22.3]
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 23.1]
jitāsano jitaśvāso jitasaṅgo jitendriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 23.2]
sthūle bhagavato rūpe manaḥ saṃdhārayeddhiyā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 23.3]
viśeṣastasya deho 'yaṃ sthaviṣṭhaśca sthavīyasām | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 24.1]
yatredaṃ vyajyate viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavacca sat | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 24.2]
aṇḍakośe śarīre 'smin saptāvaraṇasaṃyute | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 25.1]
vairājaḥ puruṣo yo 'sau bhagavān dhāraṇāśrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 25.2]
pātālam etasya hi pādamūlaṃ paṭhanti pārṣṇiprapade rasātalam | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 26.1]
mahātalaṃ viśvasṛjo 'tha gulphau talātalaṃ vai puruṣasya jaṅghe | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 26.2]
dve jānunī sutalaṃ viśvamūrter ūrudvayaṃ vitalaṃ cātalaṃ ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 27.1]
mahītalaṃ tajjaghanaṃ mahīpate nabhastalaṃ nābhisaro gṛṇanti | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 27.2]
uraḥsthalaṃ jyotiranīkam asya grīvā maharvadanaṃ vai jano 'sya | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 28.1]
tapo varāṭīṃ vidurādipuṃsaḥ satyaṃ tu śīrṣāṇi sahasraśīrṣṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 28.2]
indrādayo bāhava āhurusrāḥ karṇau diśaḥ śrotram amuṣya śabdaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 29.1]
nāsatyadasrau paramasya nāse ghrāṇo 'sya gandho mukham agniriddhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 29.2]
dyaurakṣiṇī cakṣurabhūt pataṅgaḥ pakṣmāṇi viṣṇorahanī ubhe ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 30.1]
tadbhrūvijṛmbhaḥ parameṣṭhidhiṣṇyam āpo 'sya tālū rasa eva jihvā | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 30.2]
chandāṃsyanantasya śiro gṛṇanti daṃṣṭrā yamaḥ snehakalā dvijāni | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 31.1]
hāso janonmādakarī ca māyā durantasargo yadapāṅgamokṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 31.2]
vrīḍottarauṣṭho 'dhara eva lobho dharmaḥ stano 'dharmapatho 'sya pṛṣṭham | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 32.1]
kastasya meḍhraṃ vṛṣaṇau ca mitrau kukṣiḥ samudrā girayo 'sthisaṅghāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 32.2]
nāḍyo 'sya nadyo 'tha tanūruhāṇi mahīruhā viśvatanornṛpendra | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 33.1]
anantavīryaḥ śvasitaṃ mātariśvā gatirvayaḥ karma guṇapravāhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 33.2]
īśasya keśān vidurambuvāhān vāsastu sandhyāṃ kuruvarya bhūmnaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 34.1]
avyaktam āhurhṛdayaṃ manaścasa candramāḥ sarvavikārakośaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 34.2]
vijñānaśaktiṃ mahim āmananti sarvātmano 'ntaḥkaraṇaṃ giritram | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 35.1]
aśvāśvataryuṣṭragajā nakhāni sarve mṛgāḥ paśavaḥ śroṇideśe | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 35.2]
vayāṃsi tadvyākaraṇaṃ vicitraṃ manurmanīṣā manujo nivāsaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 36.1]
gandharvavidyādharacāraṇāpsaraḥ svarasmṛtīrasurānīkavīryaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 36.2]
brahmānanaṃ kṣatrabhujo mahātmā viḍūruraṅghriśritakṛṣṇavarṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 37.1]
nānābhidhābhījyagaṇopapanno dravyātmakaḥ karma vitānayogaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 37.2]
iyān asāvīśvaravigrahasya yaḥ saṃniveśaḥ kathito mayā te | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 38.1]
saṃdhāryate 'smin vapuṣi sthaviṣṭhe manaḥ svabuddhyā na yato 'sti kiṃcit | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 38.2]
sa sarvadhīvṛttyanubhūtasarva ātmā yathā svapnajanekṣitaikaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 39.1]
taṃ satyam ānandanidhiṃ bhajeta nānyatra sajedyata ātmapātaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 1 39.2]
{BhāgPur, 2, 2}
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 1.1]
evaṃ purā dhāraṇayātmayonir naṣṭāṃ smṛtiṃ pratyavarudhya tuṣṭāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 1.2]
tathā sasarjedam amoghadṛṣṭir yathāpyayāt prāg vyavasāyabuddhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 1.3]
śābdasya hi brahmaṇa eṣa panthā yan nāmabhirdhyāyati dhīrapārthaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 2.1]
paribhramaṃstatra na vindate 'rthān māyāmaye vāsanayā śayānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 2.2]
ataḥ kavirnāmasu yāvadarthaḥ syādapramatto vyavasāyabuddhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 3.1]
siddhe 'nyathārthe na yateta tatra pariśramaṃ tatra samīkṣamāṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 3.2]
satyāṃ kṣitau kiṃ kaśipoḥ prayāsair bāhau svasiddhe hyupabarhaṇaiḥ kim | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 4.1]
satyañjalau kiṃ purudhānnapātryā digvalkalādau sati kiṃ dukūlaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 4.2]
cīrāṇi kiṃ pathi na santi diśanti bhikṣāṃ naivāṅghripāḥ parabhṛtaḥ sarito 'pyaśuṣyan | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 5.1]
ruddhā guhāḥ kim ajito 'vati nopasannān kasmādbhajanti kavayo dhanadurmadāndhān | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 5.2]
evaṃ svacitte svata eva siddha ātmā priyo 'rtho bhagavān anantaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 6.1]
taṃ nirvṛto niyatārtho bhajeta saṃsārahetūparamaśca yatra | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 6.2]
kastāṃ tv anādṛtya parānucintām ṛte paśūn asatīṃ nāma kuryāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 7.1]
paśyañ janaṃ patitaṃ vaitaraṇyāṃ svakarmajān paritāpāñ juṣāṇam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 7.2]
kecit svadehāntarhṛdayāvakāśe prādeśamātraṃ puruṣaṃ vasantam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 8.1]
caturbhujaṃ kañjarathāṅgaśaṅkhagadādharaṃ dhāraṇayā smaranti | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 8.2]
rasannavaktraṃ nalināyatekṣaṇaṃ kadambakiñjalkapiśaṅgavāsasam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 9.1]
lasanmahāratnahiraṇmayāṅgadaṃ sphuranmahāratnakirīṭakuṇḍalam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 9.2]
unnidrahṛtpaṅkajakarṇikālaye yogeśvarāsthāpitapādapallavam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 10.1]
śrīlakṣaṇaṃ kaustubharatnakandharam amlānalakṣmyā vanamālayācitam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 10.2]
vibhūṣitaṃ mekhalayāṅgulīyakair mahādhanairnūpurakaṅkaṇādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 11.1]
snigdhāmalākuñcitanīlakuntalair virocamānānanahāsapeśalam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 11.2]
adīnalīlāhasitekṣaṇollasadbhrūbhaṅgasaṃsūcitabhūryanugraham | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 12.1]
īkṣeta cintāmayam enam īśvaraṃ yāvan mano dhāraṇayāvatiṣṭhate | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 12.2]
ekaikaśo 'ṅgāni dhiyānubhāvayet pādādi yāvaddhasitaṃ gadābhṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 13.1]
jitaṃ jitaṃ sthānam apohya dhārayet paraṃ paraṃ śudhyati dhīryathā yathā | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 13.2]
yāvan na jāyeta parāvare 'smin viśveśvare draṣṭari bhaktiyogaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 14.1]
tāvat sthavīyaḥ puruṣasya rūpaṃ kriyāvasāne prayataḥ smareta | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 14.2]
sthiraṃ sukhaṃ cāsanam āsthito yatir yadā jihāsurimam aṅga lokam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 15.1]
kāle ca deśe ca mano na sajjayet prāṇān niyacchen manasā jitāsuḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 15.2]
manaḥ svabuddhyāmalayā niyamya kṣetrajña etāṃ ninayet tam ātmani | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 16.1]
ātmānam ātmanyavarudhya dhīro labdhopaśāntirvirameta kṛtyāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 16.2]
na yatra kālo 'nimiṣāṃ paraḥ prabhuḥ kuto nu devā jagatāṃ ya īśire | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 17.1]
na yatra sattvaṃ na rajastamaśca na vai vikāro na mahān pradhānam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 17.2]
paraṃ padaṃ vaiṣṇavam āmananti tad yan neti netītyatadutsisṛkṣavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 18.1]
visṛjya daurātmyam ananyasauhṛdā hṛdopaguhyārhapadaṃ pade pade | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 18.2]
itthaṃ munistūparamedvyavasthito vijñānadṛgvīryasurandhitāśayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 19.1]
svapārṣṇināpīḍya gudaṃ tato 'nilaṃ sthāneṣu ṣaṭsūnnamayej jitaklamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 19.2]
nābhyāṃ sthitaṃ hṛdyadhiropya tasmād udānagatyorasi taṃ nayen muniḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 20.1]
tato 'nusaṃdhāya dhiyā manasvī svatālumūlaṃ śanakairnayeta | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 20.2]
tasmādbhruvorantaram unnayeta niruddhasaptāyatano 'napekṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 21.1]
sthitvā muhūrtārdham akuṇṭhadṛṣṭir nirbhidya mūrdhan visṛjet paraṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 21.2]
yadi prayāsyan nṛpa pārameṣṭhyaṃ vaihāyasānām uta yadvihāram | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 22.1]
aṣṭādhipatyaṃ guṇasaṃnivāye sahaiva gacchen manasendriyaiśca | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 22.2]
yogeśvarāṇāṃ gatim āhurantar bahistrilokyāḥ pavanāntarātmanām | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 23.1]
na karmabhistāṃ gatim āpnuvanti vidyātapoyogasamādhibhājām | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 23.2]
vaiśvānaraṃ yāti vihāyasā gataḥ suṣumṇayā brahmapathena śociṣā | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 24.1]
vidhūtakalko 'tha harerudastāt prayāti cakraṃ nṛpa śaiśumāram | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 24.2]
tadviśvanābhiṃ tvativartya viṣṇor aṇīyasā virajenātmanaikaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 25.1]
namaskṛtaṃ brahmavidām upaiti kalpāyuṣo yadvibudhā ramante | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 25.2]
atho anantasya mukhānalena dandahyamānaṃ sa nirīkṣya viśvam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 26.1]
niryāti siddheśvarajuṣṭadhiṣṇyaṃ yad dvaiparārdhyaṃ tad u pārameṣṭhyam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 26.2]
na yatra śoko na jarā na mṛtyur nārtirna codvega ṛte kutaścit | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 27.1]
yaccit tato 'daḥ kṛpayānidaṃvidāṃ durantaduḥkhaprabhavānudarśanāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 27.2]
tato viśeṣaṃ pratipadya nirbhayas tenātmanāpo 'nalamūrtiratvaran | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 28.1]
jyotirmayo vāyum upetya kāle vāyvātmanā khaṃ bṛhadātmaliṅgam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 28.2]
ghrāṇena gandhaṃ rasanena vai rasaṃ rūpaṃ ca dṛṣṭyā śvasanaṃ tvacaiva | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 29.1]
śrotreṇa copetya nabhoguṇatvaṃ prāṇena cākūtim upaiti yogī | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 29.2]
sa bhūtasūkṣmendriyasannikarṣaṃ manomayaṃ devamayaṃ vikāryam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 30.1]
saṃsādya gatyā saha tena yāti vijñānatattvaṃ guṇasannirodham | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 30.2]
tenātmanātmānam upaiti śāntam ānandam ānandamayo 'vasāne | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 31.1]
etāṃ gatiṃ bhāgavatīṃ gato yaḥ sa vai punarneha viṣajjate 'ṅga | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 31.2]
ete sṛtī te nṛpa vedagīte tvayābhipṛṣṭe ca sanātane ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 32.1]
ye vai purā brahmaṇa āha tuṣṭa ārādhito bhagavān vāsudevaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 32.2]
na hyato 'nyaḥ śivaḥ panthā viśataḥ saṃsṛtāviha | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 33.1]
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogo yato bhavet | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 33.2]
bhagavān brahma kārtsnyena triranvīkṣya manīṣayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 34.1]
tadadhyavasyat kūṭastho ratirātman yato bhavet | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 34.2]
bhagavān sarvabhūteṣu lakṣitaḥ svātmanā hariḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 35.1]
dṛśyairbuddhyādibhirdraṣṭā lakṣaṇairanumāpakaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 35.2]
tasmāt sarvātmanā rājan hariḥ sarvatra sarvadā | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 36.1]
śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaśca smartavyo bhagavān nṛṇām | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 36.2]
pibanti ye bhagavata ātmanaḥ satāṃ kathāmṛtaṃ śravaṇapuṭeṣu saṃbhṛtam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 37.1]
punanti te viṣayavidūṣitāśayaṃ vrajanti taccaraṇasaroruhāntikam | [BhāgPur, 2, 2 37.2]
{BhāgPur, 2, 3}
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 1.1]
evam etan nigaditaṃ pṛṣṭavān yadbhavān mama | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 1.2]
nṛṇāṃ yan mriyamāṇānāṃ manuṣyeṣu manīṣiṇām | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 1.3]
brahmavarcasakāmastu yajeta brahmaṇaḥ patim | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 2.1]
indram indriyakāmastu prajākāmaḥ prajāpatīn | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 2.2]
devīṃ māyāṃ tu śrīkāmastejaskāmo vibhāvasum | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 3.1]
vasukāmo vasūn rudrān vīryakāmo 'tha vīryavān | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 3.2]
annādyakāmastvaditiṃ svargakāmo 'diteḥ sutān | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 4.1]
viśvān devān rājyakāmaḥ sādhyān saṃsādhako viśām | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 4.2]
āyuṣkāmo 'śvinau devau puṣṭikāma ilāṃ yajet | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 5.1]
pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ puruṣo rodasī lokamātarau | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 5.2]
rūpābhikāmo gandharvān strīkāmo 'psara urvaśīm | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 6.1]
ādhipatyakāmaḥ sarveṣāṃ yajeta parameṣṭhinam | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 6.2]
yajñaṃ yajedyaśaskāmaḥ kośakāmaḥ pracetasam | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 7.1]
vidyākāmastu giriśaṃ dāmpatyārtha umāṃ satīm | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 7.2]
dharmārtha uttamaślokaṃ tantuḥ tanvan pitṝn yajet | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 8.1]
rakṣākāmaḥ puṇyajanān ojaskāmo marudgaṇān | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 8.2]
rājyakāmo manūn devān nirṛtiṃ tvabhicaran yajet | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 9.1]
kāmakāmo yajet somam akāmaḥ puruṣaṃ param | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 9.2]
akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā mokṣakāma udāradhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 10.1]
tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena yajeta puruṣaṃ param | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 10.2]
etāvān eva yajatām iha niḥśreyasodayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 11.1]
bhagavatyacalo bhāvo yadbhāgavatasaṅgataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 11.2]
jñānaṃ yad āpratinivṛttaguṇormicakram ātmaprasāda uta yatra guṇeṣvasaṅgaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 12.1]
kaivalyasaṃmatapathastvatha bhaktiyogaḥ ko nirvṛto harikathāsu ratiṃ na kuryāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 12.2]
śaunaka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 13.1]
ityabhivyāhṛtaṃ rājā niśamya bharatarṣabhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 13.2]
kim anyat pṛṣṭavān bhūyo vaiyāsakim ṛṣiṃ kavim | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 13.3]
etacchuśrūṣatāṃ vidvan sūta no 'rhasi bhāṣitum | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 14.1]
kathā harikathodarkāḥ satāṃ syuḥ sadasi dhruvam | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 14.2]
sa vai bhāgavato rājā pāṇḍaveyo mahārathaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 15.1]
bālakrīḍanakaiḥ krīḍan kṛṣṇakrīḍāṃ ya ādade | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 15.2]
vaiyāsakiśca bhagavān vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 16.1]
urugāyaguṇodārāḥ satāṃ syurhi samāgame | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 16.2]
āyurharati vai puṃsām udyann astaṃ ca yann asau | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 17.1]
tasyarte yatkṣaṇo nīta uttamaślokavārtayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 17.2]
taravaḥ kiṃ na jīvanti bhastrāḥ kiṃ na śvasantyuta | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 18.1]
na khādanti na mehanti kiṃ grāme paśavo 'pare | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 18.2]
śvaviḍvarāhoṣṭrakharaiḥ saṃstutaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 19.1]
na yatkarṇapathopeto jātu nāma gadāgrajaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 19.2]
bile batorukramavikramān ye na śṛṇvataḥ karṇapuṭe narasya | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 20.1]
jihvāsatī dārdurikeva sūta na copagāyatyurugāyagāthāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 20.2]
bhāraḥ paraṃ paṭṭakirīṭajuṣṭam apyuttamāṅgaṃ na namen mukundam | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 21.1]
śāvau karau no kurute saparyāṃ harerlasatkāñcanakaṅkaṇau vā | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 21.2]
barhāyite te nayane narāṇāṃ liṅgāni viṣṇorna nirīkṣato ye | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 22.1]
pādau nṛṇāṃ tau drumajanmabhājau kṣetrāṇi nānuvrajato hareryau | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 22.2]
jīvañchavo bhāgavatāṅghrireṇuṃ na jātu martyo 'bhilabheta yastu | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 23.1]
śrīviṣṇupadyā manujastulasyāḥ śvasañchavo yastu na veda gandham | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 23.2]
tadaśmasāraṃ hṛdayaṃ batedaṃ yadgṛhyamāṇairharināmadheyaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 24.1]
na vikriyetātha yadā vikāro netre jalaṃ gātraruheṣu harṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 24.2]
athābhidhehyaṅga mano'nukūlaṃ prabhāṣase bhāgavatapradhānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 25.1]
yadāha vaiyāsakirātmavidyāviśārado nṛpatiṃ sādhu pṛṣṭaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 3 25.2]
{BhāgPur, 2, 4}
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 1.1]
vaiyāsakeriti vacastattvaniścayam ātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 1.2]
upadhārya matiṃ kṛṣṇe auttareyaḥ satīṃ vyadhāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 1.3]
ātmajāyāsutāgārapaśudraviṇabandhuṣu | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 2.1]
rājye cāvikale nityaṃ virūḍhāṃ mamatāṃ jahau | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 2.2]
papraccha cemam evārthaṃ yan māṃ pṛcchatha sattamāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 3.1]
kṛṣṇānubhāvaśravaṇe śraddadhāno mahāmanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 3.2]
saṃsthāṃ vijñāya saṃnyasya karma traivargikaṃ ca yat | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 4.1]
vāsudeve bhagavati ātmabhāvaṃ dṛḍhaṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 4.2]
rājovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 5.1]
samīcīnaṃ vaco brahman sarvajñasya tavānagha | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 5.2]
tamo viśīryate mahyaṃ hareḥ kathayataḥ kathām | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 5.3]
bhūya eva vivitsāmi bhagavān ātmamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 6.1]
yathedaṃ sṛjate viśvaṃ durvibhāvyam adhīśvaraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 6.2]
yathā gopāyati vibhuryathā saṃyacchate punaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 7.1]
yāṃ yāṃ śaktim upāśritya puruśaktiḥ paraḥ pumān | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 7.2]
ātmānaṃ krīḍayan krīḍan karoti vikaroti ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 7.3]
nūnaṃ bhagavato brahman hareradbhutakarmaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 8.1]
durvibhāvyam ivābhāti kavibhiścāpi ceṣṭitam | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 8.2]
yathā guṇāṃstu prakṛteryugapat kramaśo 'pi vā | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 9.1]
bibharti bhūriśastvekaḥ kurvan karmāṇi janmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 9.2]
vicikitsitam etan me bravītu bhagavān yathā | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 10.1]
śābde brahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ parasmiṃśca bhavān khalu | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 10.2]
sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 11.1]
ityupāmantrito rājñā guṇānukathane hareḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 11.2]
hṛṣīkeśam anusmṛtya prativaktuṃ pracakrame | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 11.3]
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 12.1]
namaḥ parasmai puruṣāya bhūyase sadudbhavasthānanirodhalīlayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 12.2]
gṛhītaśaktitritayāya dehinām antarbhavāyānupalakṣyavartmane | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 12.3]
bhūyo namaḥ sadvṛjinacchide 'satām asambhavāyākhilasattvamūrtaye | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 13.1]
puṃsāṃ punaḥ pāramahaṃsya āśrame vyavasthitānām anumṛgyadāśuṣe | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 13.2]
namo namaste 'stvṛṣabhāya sātvatāṃ vidūrakāṣṭhāya muhuḥ kuyoginām | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 14.1]
nirastasāmyātiśayena rādhasā svadhāmani brahmaṇi raṃsyate namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 14.2]
yatkīrtanaṃ yatsmaraṇaṃ yadīkṣaṇaṃ yadvandanaṃ yacchravaṇaṃ yadarhaṇam | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 15.1]
lokasya sadyo vidhunoti kalmaṣaṃ tasmai subhadraśravase namo namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 15.2]
vicakṣaṇā yaccaraṇopasādanāt saṅgaṃ vyudasyobhayato 'ntarātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 16.1]
vindanti hi brahmagatiṃ gataklamāstasmai subhadraśravase namo namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 16.2]
tapasvino dānaparā yaśasvino manasvino mantravidaḥ sumaṅgalāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 17.1]
kṣemaṃ na vindanti vinā yadarpaṇaṃ tasmai subhadraśravase namo namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 17.2]
kirātahūṇāndhrapulindapulkaśā ābhīraśumbhā yavanāḥ khasādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 18.1]
ye 'nye ca pāpā yadapāśrayāśrayāḥ śudhyanti tasmai prabhaviṣṇave namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 18.2]
sa eṣa ātmātmavatām adhīśvarastrayīmayo dharmamayastapomayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 19.1]
gatavyalīkairajaśaṅkarādibhirvitarkyaliṅgo bhagavān prasīdatām | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 19.2]
śriyaḥ patiryajñapatiḥ prajāpatirdhiyāṃ patirlokapatirdharāpatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 20.1]
patirgatiścāndhakavṛṣṇisātvatāṃ prasīdatāṃ me bhagavān satāṃ patiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 20.2]
yadaṅghryabhidhyānasamādhidhautayā dhiyānupaśyanti hi tattvam ātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 21.1]
vadanti caitat kavayo yathārucaṃ sa me mukundo bhagavān prasīdatām | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 21.2]
pracoditā yena purā sarasvatī vitanvatājasya satīṃ smṛtiṃ hṛdi | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 22.1]
svalakṣaṇā prādurabhūt kilāsyataḥ sa me ṛṣīṇām ṛṣabhaḥ prasīdatām | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 22.2]
bhūtairmahadbhirya imāḥ puro vibhurnirmāya śete yadamūṣu pūruṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 23.1]
bhuṅkte guṇān ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśātmakaḥ so 'laṃkṛṣīṣṭa bhagavān vacāṃsi me | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 23.2]
namastasmai bhagavate vāsudevāya vedhase | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 24.1]
papurjñānamayaṃ saumyā yanmukhāmburuhāsavam | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 24.2]
etadevātmabhū rājan nāradāya vipṛcchate | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 25.1]
vedagarbho 'bhyadhāt sākṣādyadāha harirātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 4 25.2]
{BhāgPur, 2, 5}
nārada uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 1.1]
devadeva namaste 'stu bhūtabhāvana pūrvaja | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 1.2]
tadvijānīhi yaj jñānam ātmatattvanidarśanam | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 1.3]
yadrūpaṃ yadadhiṣṭhānaṃ yataḥ sṛṣṭam idaṃ prabho | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 2.1]
yatsaṃsthaṃ yat paraṃ yac ca tat tattvaṃ vada tattvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 2.2]
sarvaṃ hyetadbhavān veda bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 3.1]
karāmalakavadviśvaṃ vijñānāvasitaṃ tava | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 3.2]
yadvijñāno yadādhāro yatparastvaṃ yadātmakaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 4.1]
ekaḥ sṛjasi bhūtāni bhūtairevātmamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 4.2]
ātman bhāvayase tāni na parābhāvayan svayam | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 5.1]
ātmaśaktim avaṣṭabhya ūrṇanābhirivāklamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 5.2]
nāhaṃ veda paraṃ hyasmin nāparaṃ na samaṃ vibho | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 6.1]
nāmarūpaguṇairbhāvyaṃ sadasat kiṃcidanyataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 6.2]
sa bhavān acaradghoraṃ yat tapaḥ susamāhitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 7.1]
tena khedayase nastvaṃ parāśaṅkāṃ ca yacchasi | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 7.2]
etan me pṛcchataḥ sarvaṃ sarvajña sakaleśvara | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 8.1]
vijānīhi yathaivedam ahaṃ budhye 'nuśāsitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 8.2]
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 9.1]
samyak kāruṇikasyedaṃ vatsa te vicikitsitam | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 9.2]
yadahaṃ coditaḥ saumya bhagavadvīryadarśane | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 9.3]
nānṛtaṃ tava tac cāpi yathā māṃ prabravīṣi bhoḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 10.1]
avijñāya paraṃ matta etāvat tvaṃ yato hi me | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 10.2]
yena svarociṣā viśvaṃ rocitaṃ rocayāmyaham | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 11.1]
yathārko 'gniryathā somo yatharkṣagrahatārakāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 11.2]
tasmai namo bhagavate vāsudevāya dhīmahi | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 12.1]
yanmāyayā durjayayā māṃ vadanti jagadgurum | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 12.2]
vilajjamānayā yasya sthātum īkṣāpathe 'muyā | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 13.1]
vimohitā vikatthante mamāham iti durdhiyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 13.2]
dravyaṃ karma ca kālaśca svabhāvo jīva eva ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 14.1]
vāsudevāt paro brahman na cānyo 'rtho 'sti tattvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 14.2]
nārāyaṇaparā vedā devā nārāyaṇāṅgajāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 15.1]
nārāyaṇaparā lokā nārāyaṇaparā makhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 15.2]
nārāyaṇaparo yogo nārāyaṇaparaṃ tapaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 16.1]
nārāyaṇaparaṃ jñānaṃ nārāyaṇaparā gatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 16.2]
tasyāpi draṣṭurīśasya kūṭasthasyākhilātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 17.1]
sṛjyaṃ sṛjāmi sṛṣṭo 'ham īkṣayaivābhicoditaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 17.2]
sattvaṃ rajastama iti nirguṇasya guṇāstrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 18.1]
sthitisarganirodheṣu gṛhītā māyayā vibhoḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 18.2]
kāryakāraṇakartṛtve dravyajñānakriyāśrayāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 19.1]
badhnanti nityadā muktaṃ māyinaṃ puruṣaṃ guṇāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 19.2]
sa eṣa bhagavāṃl liṅgaistribhiretairadhokṣajaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 20.1]
svalakṣitagatirbrahman sarveṣāṃ mama ceśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 20.2]
kālaṃ karma svabhāvaṃ ca māyeśo māyayā svayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 21.1]
ātman yadṛcchayā prāptaṃ vibubhūṣurupādade | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 21.2]
kālādguṇavyatikaraḥ pariṇāmaḥ svabhāvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 22.1]
karmaṇo janma mahataḥ puruṣādhiṣṭhitādabhūt | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 22.2]
mahatastu vikurvāṇādrajaḥsattvopabṛṃhitāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 23.1]
tamaḥpradhānastvabhavaddravyajñānakriyātmakaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 23.2]
so 'haṅkāra iti prokto vikurvan samabhūt tridhā | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 24.1]
vaikārikastaijasaśca tāmasaśceti yadbhidā | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 24.2]
dravyaśaktiḥ kriyāśaktir jñānaśaktiriti prabho | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 24.3]
tāmasādapi bhūtādervikurvāṇādabhūn nabhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 25.1]
tasya mātrā guṇaḥ śabdo liṅgaṃ yaddraṣṭṛdṛśyayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 25.2]
nabhaso 'tha vikurvāṇādabhūt sparśaguṇo 'nilaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 5 26.1]

{BhāgPur, 2, 6}
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 1.1]
vācāṃ vahnermukhaṃ kṣetraṃ chandasāṃ sapta dhātavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 1.2]

ahaṃ bhavān bhavaścaiva ta ime munayo 'grajāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 12.1]
surāsuranarā nāgāḥ khagā mṛgasarīsṛpāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 12.2]
gandharvāpsaraso yakṣā rakṣobhūtagaṇoragāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 13.1]
paśavaḥ pitaraḥ siddhā vidyādhrāścāraṇā drumāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 13.2]
anye ca vividhā jīvā jalasthalanabhaukasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 14.1]
graharkṣaketavastārāstaḍitaḥ stanayitnavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 14.2]
sarvaṃ puruṣa evedaṃ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavac ca yat | [BhāgPur, 2, 6 15.1]

{BhāgPur, 2, 7}
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 1.1]

satre mamāsa bhagavān hayaśīraṣātho sākṣāt sa yajñapuruṣastapanīyavarṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 11.1]

jñānaṃ ca bhāgavatam ātmasatattvadīpaṃ yadvāsudevaśaraṇā vidurañjasaiva | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 19.2]

tiṣṭhan vanaṃ sadayitānuja āviveśa yasmin virudhya daśakandhara ārtim ārchat | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 23.2]

tacchuddhaye 'tiviṣavīryavilolajihvamuccāṭayiṣyaduragaṃ viharan hradinyām | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 28.2]

yāsyantyadarśanam alaṃ balapārthabhīmavyājāhvayena hariṇā nilayaṃ tadīyam | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 35.2]

svāhā svadhā vaṣaḍiti sma giro na yatra śāstā bhaviṣyati kalerbhagavān yugānte | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 38.2]

māndhātralarkaśatadhanvanurantidevā devavrato baliramūrtarayo dilīpaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 7 44.2]

rājovāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 1.1]
brahmaṇā codito brahman guṇākhyāne 'guṇasya ca | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 1.2]
yasmai yasmai yathā prāha nārado devadarśanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 1.3]
etadveditum icchāmi tattvaṃ tattvavidāṃ vara | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 2.1]
hareradbhutavīryasya kathā lokasumaṅgalāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 2.2]
kathayasva mahābhāga yathāham akhilātmani | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 3.1]
kṛṣṇe niveśya niḥsaṅgaṃ manastyakṣye kalevaram | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 3.2]

yadṛcchayā hetunā vā bhavanto jānate yathā | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 7.2]
āsīdyadudarāt padmaṃ lokasaṃsthānalakṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 8.1]
yāvān ayaṃ vai puruṣa iyattāvayavaiḥ pṛthak | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 8.2]
tāvān asāviti proktaḥ saṃsthāvayavavān iva | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 8.3]
ajaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni bhūtātmā yadanugrahāt | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 9.1]
dadṛśe yena tadrūpaṃ nābhipadmasamudbhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 9.2]

yāvān kalpo vikalpo vā yathā kālo 'numīyate | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 12.1]
bhūtabhavyabhavacchabda āyurmānaṃ ca yat sataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 12.2]
kālasyānugatiryā tu lakṣyate 'ṇvī bṛhatyapi | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 13.1]
yāvatyaḥ karmagatayo yādṛśīrdvijasattama | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 13.2]
yasmin karmasamāvāyo yathā yenopagṛhyate | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 14.1]
guṇānāṃ guṇināṃ caiva pariṇāmam abhīpsatām | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 14.2]
bhūpātālakakubvyomagrahanakṣatrabhūbhṛtām | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 15.1]
saritsamudradvīpānāṃ sambhavaścaitadokasām | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 15.2]
pramāṇam aṇḍakośasya bāhyābhyantarabhedataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 16.1]
mahatāṃ cānucaritaṃ varṇāśramaviniścayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 16.2]
yugāni yugamānaṃ ca dharmo yaśca yuge yuge | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 17.1]
avatārānucaritaṃ yadāścaryatamaṃ hareḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 17.2]

tattvānāṃ parisaṅkhyānaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hetulakṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 19.1]

yogeśvaraiśvaryagatirliṅgabhaṅgastu yoginām | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 20.1]
vedopavedadharmāṇām itihāsapurāṇayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 20.2]
samplavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vikramaḥ pratisaṅkramaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 21.1]

ātmano bandhamokṣau ca vyavasthānaṃ svarūpataḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 22.2]
yathātmatantro bhagavān vikrīḍatyātmamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 23.1]
visṛjya vā yathā māyām udāste sākṣivadvibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 23.2]

tattvato 'rhasyudāhartuṃ prapannāya mahāmune | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 24.2]

sūta uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 27.1]
sa upāmantrito rājñā kathāyām iti satpateḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 27.2]
brahmarāto bhṛśaṃ prīto viṣṇurātena saṃsadi | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 27.3]
prāha bhāgavataṃ nāma purāṇaṃ brahmasaṃmitam | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 28.1]
brahmaṇe bhagavatproktaṃ brahmakalpa upāgate | [BhāgPur, 2, 8 28.2]

{BhāgPur, 2, 9}
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 1.1]
ātmamāyām ṛte rājan parasyānubhavātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 1.2]
na ghaṭetārthasambandhaḥ svapnadraṣṭurivāñjasā | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 1.3]
bahurūpa ivābhāti māyayā bahurūpayā | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 2.1]
ramamāṇo guṇeṣvasyā mamāham iti manyate | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 2.2]
yarhi vāva mahimni sve parasmin kālamāyayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 3.1]
rameta gatasammohastyaktvodāste tadobhayam | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 3.2]
ātmatattvaviśuddhyarthaṃ yadāha bhagavān ṛtam | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 4.1]
brahmaṇe darśayan rūpam avyalīkavratādṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 4.2]

tāṃ nādhyagacchaddṛśam atra saṃmatāṃ prapañcanirmāṇavidhiryayā bhavet | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 5.2]

sparśeṣu yat ṣoḍaśam ekaviṃśaṃ niṣkiñcanānāṃ nṛpa yaddhanaṃ viduḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 6.2]
niśamya tadvaktṛdidṛkṣayā diśo vilokya tatrānyadapaśyamānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 7.1]

pravartate yatra rajastamastayoḥ sattvaṃ ca miśraṃ na ca kālavikramaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 10.1]
na yatra māyā kim utāpare harer anuvratā yatra surāsurārcitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 10.2]
śyāmāvadātāḥ śatapatralocanāḥ piśaṅgavastrāḥ surucaḥ supeśasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 11.1]
sarve caturbāhava unmiṣanmaṇipravekaniṣkābharaṇāḥ suvarcasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 11.2]
pravālavaidūryamṛṇālavarcasaḥ parisphuratkuṇḍalamaulimālinaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 11.3]
bhrājiṣṇubhiryaḥ parito virājate lasadvimānāvalibhirmahātmanām | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 12.1]
vidyotamānaḥ pramadottamādyubhiḥ savidyudabhrāvalibhiryathā nabhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 12.2]
śrīryatra rūpiṇyurugāyapādayoḥ karoti mānaṃ bahudhā vibhūtibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 13.1]
preṅkhaṃ śritā yā kusumākarānugair vigīyamānā priyakarma gāyatī | [BhāgPur, 2, 9 13.2]

yadā tu rājā svasutān asādhūn puṣṇan na dharmeṇa vinaṣṭadṛṣṭiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 6.2]
bhrātur yaviṣṭhasya sutān vibandhūn praveśya lākṣābhavane dadāha | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 6.3]
yadā sabhāyāṃ kurudevadevyāḥ keśābhimarśaṃ sutakarma garhyam | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 7.1]
na vārayāmāsa nṛpaḥ snuṣāyāḥ svāsrair harantyāḥ kucakuṅkumāni | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 7.2]
dyūte tv adharmeṇa jitasya sādhoḥ satyāvalambasya vanaṃ gatasya | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 8.1]
na yācato 'dāt samayena dāyaṃ tamojuṣāṇo yad ajātaśatroḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 8.2]
yadā ca pārthaprahitaḥ sabhāyāṃ jagadgurur yāni jagāda kṛṣṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 9.1]
na tāni puṃsām amṛtāyanāni rājoru mene kṣatapuṇyaleśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 9.2]
yadopahūto bhavanaṃ praviṣṭo mantrāya pṛṣṭaḥ kila pūrvajena | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 10.1]
athāha tan mantradṛśāṃ varīyān yan mantriṇo vaidurikaṃ vadanti | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 10.2]
ajātaśatroḥ pratiyaccha dāyaṃ titikṣato durviṣahaṃ tavāgaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 11.1]
sahānujo yatra vṛkodarāhiḥ śvasan ruṣā yat tvam alaṃ bibheṣi | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 11.2]
pārthāṃs tu devo bhagavān mukundo gṛhītavān sakṣitidevadevaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 12.1]
āste svapuryāṃ yadudevadevo vinirjitāśeṣanṛdevadevaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 12.2]
sa eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣadviḍ āste gṛhān praviṣṭo yam apatyamatyā | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 13.1]
puṣṇāsi kṛṣṇād vimukho gataśrīs tyajāśv aśaivaṃ kulakauśalāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 13.2]
ity ūcivāṃs tatra suyodhanena pravṛddhakopasphuritādhareṇa | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 14.1]
asatkṛtaḥ satspṛhaṇīyaśīlaḥ kṣattā sakarṇānujasaubalena | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 14.2]
ka enam atropajuhāva jihmaṃ dāsyāḥ sutaṃ yadbalinaiva puṣṭaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 15.1]
tasmin pratīpaḥ parakṛtya āste nirvāsyatām āśu purāc chvasānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 15.2]
svayaṃ dhanur dvāri nidhāya māyāṃ bhrātuḥ puro marmasu tāḍito 'pi | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 16.1]
sa ittham atyulbaṇakarṇabāṇair gatavyatho 'yād uru mānayānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 16.2]
sa nirgataḥ kauravapuṇyalabdho gajāhvayāt tīrthapadaḥ padāni | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 17.1]
anvākramat puṇyacikīrṣayorvyām adhiṣṭhito yāni sahasramūrtiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 17.2]
pureṣu puṇyopavanādrikuñjeṣv apaṅkatoyeṣu saritsaraḥsu | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 18.1]
anantaliṅgaiḥ samalaṃkṛteṣu cacāra tīrthāyataneṣv ananyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 18.2]
gāṃ paryaṭan medhyaviviktavṛttiḥ sadāpluto 'dhaḥ śayano 'vadhūtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 19.1]
alakṣitaḥ svair avadhūtaveṣo vratāni cere haritoṣaṇāni | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 19.2]
itthaṃ vrajan bhāratam eva varṣaṃ kālena yāvad gatavān prabhāsam | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 20.1]
tāvac chaśāsa kṣitim eka cakrāml ekātapatrām ajitena pārthaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 20.2]
tatrātha śuśrāva suhṛdvinaṣṭiṃ vanaṃ yathā veṇujavahnisaṃśrayam | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 21.1]
saṃspardhayā dagdham athānuśocan sarasvatīṃ pratyag iyāya tūṣṇīm | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 21.2]
tasyāṃ tritasyośanaso manoś ca pṛthor athāgner asitasya vāyoḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 22.1]
tīrthaṃ sudāsasya gavāṃ guhasya yac chrāddhadevasya sa āsiṣeve | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 22.2]
anyāni ceha dvijadevadevaiḥ kṛtāni nānāyatanāni viṣṇoḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 23.1]
pratyaṅgamukhyāṅkitamandirāṇi yaddarśanāt kṛṣṇam anusmaranti | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 23.2]
tatas tv ativrajya surāṣṭram ṛddhaṃ sauvīramatsyān kurujāṅgalāṃś ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 24.1]
kālena tāvad yamunām upetya tatroddhavaṃ bhāgavataṃ dadarśa | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 24.2]
sa vāsudevānucaraṃ praśāntaṃ bṛhaspateḥ prāk tanayaṃ pratītam | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 25.1]
āliṅgya gāḍhaṃ praṇayena bhadraṃ svānām apṛcchad bhagavatprajānām | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 25.2]
kaccit purāṇau puruṣau svanābhyapādmānuvṛttyeha kilāvatīrṇau | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 26.1]
āsāta urvyāḥ kuśalaṃ vidhāya kṛtakṣaṇau kuśalaṃ śūragehe | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 26.2]
kaccit kurūṇāṃ paramaḥ suhṛn no bhāmaḥ sa āste sukham aṅga śauriḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 27.1]
yo vai svasṇāṃ pitṛvad dadāti varān vadānyo varatarpaṇena | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 27.2]
kaccid varūthādhipatir yadūnāṃ pradyumna āste sukham aṅga vīraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 28.1]
yaṃ rukmiṇī bhagavato 'bhilebhe ārādhya viprān smaram ādisarge | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 28.2]
kaccit sukhaṃ sātvatavṛṣṇibhojadāśārhakāṇām adhipaḥ sa āste | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 29.1]
yam abhyaṣiñcac chatapattranetro nṛpāsanāśāṃ parihṛtya dūrāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 29.2]
kacciddhareḥ saumya sutaḥ sadṛkṣa āste 'graṇī rathināṃ sādhu sāmbaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 30.1]
asūta yaṃ jāmbavatī vratāḍhyā devaṃ guhaṃ yo 'mbikayā dhṛto 'gre | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 30.2]
kṣemaṃ sa kaccid yuyudhāna āste yaḥ phālgunāl labdhadhanūrahasyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 31.1]
lebhe 'ñjasādhokṣajasevayaiva gatiṃ tadīyāṃ yatibhir durāpām | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 31.2]
kaccid budhaḥ svasty anamīva āste śvaphalkaputro bhagavatprapannaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 32.1]
yaḥ kṛṣṇapādāṅkitamārgapāṃsuṣv aceṣṭata premavibhinnadhairyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 32.2]
kaccic chivaṃ devakabhojaputryā viṣṇuprajāyā iva devamātuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 33.1]
yā vai svagarbheṇa dadhāra devaṃ trayī yathā yajñavitānam artham | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 33.2]
apisvid āste bhagavān sukhaṃ vo yaḥ sātvatāṃ kāmadugho 'niruddhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 34.1]
yam āmananti sma hi śabdayoniṃ manomayaṃ sattvaturīyatattvam | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 34.2]
apisvid anye ca nijātmadaivam ananyavṛttyā samanuvratā ye | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 35.1]
hṛdīkasatyātmajacārudeṣṇagadādayaḥ svasti caranti saumya | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 35.2]
api svadorbhyāṃ vijayācyutābhyāṃ dharmeṇa dharmaḥ paripāti setum | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 36.1]
duryodhano 'tapyata yatsabhāyāṃ sāmrājyalakṣmyā vijayānuvṛttyā | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 36.2]
kiṃ vā kṛtāgheṣv agham atyamarṣī bhīmo 'hivad dīrghatamaṃ vyamuñcat | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 37.1]
yasyāṅghripātaṃ raṇabhūr na sehe mārgaṃ gadāyāś carato vicitram | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 37.2]
kaccid yaśodhā rathayūthapānāṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvoparatārir āste | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 38.1]
alakṣito yaccharakūṭagūḍho māyākirāto giriśas tutoṣa | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 38.2]
yamāv utasvit tanayau pṛthāyāḥ pārthair vṛtau pakṣmabhir akṣiṇīva | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 39.1]
remāta uddāya mṛdhe svarikthaṃ parāt suparṇāv iva vajrivaktrāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 39.2]
aho pṛthāpi dhriyate 'rbhakārthe rājarṣivaryeṇa vināpi tena | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 40.1]
yas tv ekavīro 'dhiratho vijigye dhanur dvitīyaḥ kakubhaś catasraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 40.2]
saumyānuśoce tam adhaḥpatantaṃ bhrātre paretāya vidudruhe yaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 41.1]
niryāpito yena suhṛt svapuryā ahaṃ svaputrān samanuvratena | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 41.2]
so 'haṃ harer martyaviḍambanena dṛśo nṛṇāṃ cālayato vidhātuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 42.1]
nānyopalakṣyaḥ padavīṃ prasādāc carāmi paśyan gatavismayo 'tra | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 42.2]
nūnaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ trimadotpathānāṃ mahīṃ muhuś cālayatāṃ camūbhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 43.1]
vadhāt prapannārtijihīrṣayeśo 'py upaikṣatāghaṃ bhagavān kurūṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 43.2]
ajasya janmotpathanāśanāya karmāṇy akartur grahaṇāya puṃsām | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 44.1]
nanv anyathā ko 'rhati dehayogaṃ paro guṇānām uta karmatantram | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 44.2]
tasya prapannākhilalokapānām avasthitānām anuśāsane sve | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 45.1]
arthāya jātasya yaduṣv ajasya vārttāṃ sakhe kīrtaya tīrthakīrteḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 1 45.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 2}
śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 1.1]
iti bhāgavataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṣattrā vārttāṃ priyāśrayām | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 1.2]
prativaktuṃ na cotseha autkaṇṭhyāt smāriteśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 1.3]
yaḥ pañcahāyano mātrā prātarāśāya yācitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 2.1]
tan naicchad racayan yasya saparyāṃ bālalīlayā | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 2.2]
sa kathaṃ sevayā tasya kālena jarasaṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 3.1]
pṛṣṭo vārttāṃ pratibrūyād bhartuḥ pādāv anusmaran | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 3.2]
sa muhūrtam abhūt tūṣṇīṃ kṛṣṇāṅghrisudhayā bhṛśam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 4.1]
tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena nimagnaḥ sādhu nirvṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 4.2]
pulakodbhinnasarvāṅgo muñcan mīladdṛśā śucaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 5.1]
pūrṇārtho lakṣitas tena snehaprasarasaṃplutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 5.2]
śanakair bhagavallokān nṛlokaṃ punar āgataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 6.1]
vimṛjya netre viduraṃ prītyāhoddhava utsmayan | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 6.2]
uddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 7.1]
kṛṣṇadyumaṇi nimloce gīrṇeṣv ajagareṇa ha | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 7.2]
kiṃ nu naḥ kuśalaṃ brūyāṃ gataśrīṣu gṛheṣv aham | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 7.3]
durbhago bata loko 'yaṃ yadavo nitarām api | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 8.1]
ye saṃvasanto na vidur hariṃ mīnā ivoḍupam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 8.2]
iṅgitajñāḥ puruprauḍhā ekārāmāś ca sātvatāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 9.1]
sātvatām ṛṣabhaṃ sarve bhūtāvāsam amaṃsata | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 9.2]
devasya māyayā spṛṣṭā ye cānyad asadāśritāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 10.1]
bhrāmyate dhīr na tadvākyair ātmany uptātmano harau | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 10.2]
pradarśyātaptatapasām avitṛptadṛśāṃ nṛṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 11.1]
ādāyāntar adhād yas tu svabimbaṃ lokalocanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 11.2]
yan martyalīlaupayikaṃ svayogamāyābalaṃ darśayatā gṛhītam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 12.1]
vismāpanaṃ svasya ca saubhagarddheḥ paraṃ padaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣaṇāṅgam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 12.2]
yad dharmasūnor bata rājasūye nirīkṣya dṛksvastyayanaṃ trilokaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 13.1]
kārtsnyena cādyeha gataṃ vidhātur arvāksṛtau kauśalam ity amanyata | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 13.2]
vrajastriyo dṛgbhir anupravṛttadhiyo 'vatasthuḥ kila kṛtyaśeṣāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 14.2]
svaśāntarūpeṣv itaraiḥ svarūpair abhyardyamāneṣv anukampitātmā | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 15.1]
parāvareśo mahadaṃśayukto hy ajo 'pi jāto bhagavān yathāgniḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 15.2]
māṃ khedayaty etad ajasya janmaviḍambanaṃ yad vasudevagehe | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 16.1]
vraje ca vāso 'ribhayād iva svayaṃ purād vyavātsīd yadanantavīryaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 16.2]
dunoti cetaḥ smarato mamaitad yad āha pādāv abhivandya pitroḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 17.1]
tātāmba kaṃsād uruśaṅkitānāṃ prasīdataṃ no 'kṛtaniṣkṛtīnām | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 17.2]
ko vā amuṣyāṅghrisarojareṇuṃ vismartum īśīta pumān vijighran | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 18.1]
yo visphuradbhrūviṭapena bhūmer bhāraṃ kṛtāntena tiraścakāra | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 18.2]
dṛṣṭā bhavadbhir nanu rājasūye caidyasya kṛṣṇaṃ dviṣato 'pi siddhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 19.1]
yāṃ yoginaḥ saṃspṛhayanti samyag yogena kas tadvirahaṃ saheta | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 19.2]
tathaiva cānye naralokavīrā ya āhave kṛṣṇamukhāravindam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 20.1]
netraiḥ pibanto nayanābhirāmaṃ pārthāstrapūtaḥ padam āpur asya | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 20.2]
svayaṃ tv asāmyātiśayas tryadhīśaḥ svārājyalakṣmyāptasamastakāmaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 21.1]
baliṃ haradbhiś ciralokapālaiḥ kirīṭakoṭyeḍitapādapīṭhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 21.2]
tat tasya kaiṃkaryam alaṃ bhṛtān no viglāpayaty aṅga yad ugrasenam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 22.1]
tiṣṭhan niṣaṇṇaṃ parameṣṭhidhiṣṇye nyabodhayad deva nidhārayeti | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 22.2]
aho bakī yaṃ stanakālakūṭaṃ jighāṃsayāpāyayad apy asādhvī | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 23.1]
lebhe gatiṃ dhātryucitāṃ tato 'nyaṃ kaṃ vā dayāluṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajema | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 23.2]
manye 'surān bhāgavatāṃs tryadhīśe saṃrambhamārgābhiniviṣṭacittān | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 24.1]
ye saṃyuge 'cakṣata tārkṣyaputram aṃse sunābhāyudham āpatantam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 24.2]
vasudevasya devakyāṃ jāto bhojendrabandhane | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 25.1]
cikīrṣur bhagavān asyāḥ śam ajenābhiyācitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 25.2]
tato nandavrajam itaḥ pitrā kaṃsād vibibhyatā | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 26.1]
ekādaśa samās tatra gūḍhārciḥ sabalo 'vasat | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 26.2]
parīto vatsapair vatsāṃś cārayan vyaharad vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 27.1]
yamunopavane kūjaddvijasaṃkulitāṅghripe | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 27.2]
kaumārīṃ darśayaṃś ceṣṭāṃ prekṣaṇīyāṃ vrajaukasām | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 28.1]
rudann iva hasan mugdhabālasiṃhāvalokanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 28.2]
sa eva godhanaṃ lakṣmyā niketaṃ sitagovṛṣam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 29.1]
cārayann anugān gopān raṇadveṇur arīramat | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 29.2]
prayuktān bhojarājena māyinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 30.1]
līlayā vyanudat tāṃs tān bālaḥ krīḍanakān iva | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 30.2]
vipannān viṣapānena nigṛhya bhujagādhipam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 31.1]
utthāpyāpāyayad gāvas tat toyaṃ prakṛtisthitam | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 31.2]
ayājayad gosavena goparājaṃ dvijottamaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 32.1]
vittasya corubhārasya cikīrṣan sadvyayaṃ vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 32.2]
varṣatīndre vrajaḥ kopād bhagnamāne 'tivihvalaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 33.1]
gotralīlātapatreṇa trāto bhadrānugṛhṇatā | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 33.2]
śaracchaśikarair mṛṣṭaṃ mānayan rajanīmukham | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 34.1]
gāyan kalapadaṃ reme strīṇāṃ maṇḍalamaṇḍanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 2 34.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 3}
uddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 1.1]
tataḥ sa āgatya puraṃ svapitroś cikīrṣayā śaṃ baladevasaṃyutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 1.2]
nipātya tuṅgād ripuyūthanāthaṃ hataṃ vyakarṣad vyasum ojasorvyām | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 1.3]
sāṃdīpaneḥ sakṛt proktaṃ brahmādhītya savistaram | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 2.1]
tasmai prādād varaṃ putraṃ mṛtaṃ pañcajanodarāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 2.2]
samāhutā bhīṣmakakanyayā ye śriyaḥ savarṇena bubhūṣayaiṣām | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 3.1]
gāndharvavṛttyā miṣatāṃ svabhāgaṃ jahre padaṃ mūrdhni dadhat suparṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 3.2]
kakudmino 'viddhanaso damitvā svayaṃvare nāgnajitīm uvāha | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 4.1]
tadbhagnamānān api gṛdhyato 'jñāñ jaghne 'kṣataḥ śastrabhṛtaḥ svaśastraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 4.2]
priyaṃ prabhur grāmya iva priyāyā vidhitsur ārcchad dyutaruṃ yadarthe | [BhāgPur, 3, 3 5.1]

{BhāgPur, 3, 7}

pāṣaṇḍapathavaiṣamyaṃ pratilomaniveśanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 31.1]

dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ nimittāny avirodhataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 32.1]
vārttāyā daṇḍanīteś ca śrutasya ca vidhiṃ pṛthak | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 32.2]
śrāddhasya ca vidhiṃ brahman pitṝṇāṃ sargam eva ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 33.1]
grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ kālāvayavasaṃsthitim | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 33.2]
dānasya tapaso vāpi yac ceṣṭāpūrtayoḥ phalam | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 34.1]
pravāsasthasya yo dharmo yaś ca puṃsa utāpadi | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 34.2]

samprasīdati vā yeṣām etad ākhyāhi me 'nagha | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 35.2]
anuvratānāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ putrāṇāṃ ca dvijottama | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 36.1]

jñānaṃ ca naigamaṃ yat tad guruśiṣyaprayojanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 38.2]
nimittāni ca tasyeha proktāny anaghasūribhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 7 39.1]

{BhāgPur, 3, 9}
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 1.1]
jñāto 'si me 'dya sucirān nanu dehabhājāṃ na jñāyate bhagavato gatir ity avadyam | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 1.2]
nānyat tvad asti bhagavann api tan na śuddhaṃ māyāguṇavyatikarād yad urur vibhāsi | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 1.3]
rūpaṃ yad etad avabodharasodayena śaśvannivṛttatamasaḥ sadanugrahāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 2.1]
ādau gṛhītam avatāraśataikabījaṃ yan nābhipadmabhavanād aham āvirāsam | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 2.2]
nātaḥ paraṃ parama yad bhavataḥ svarūpam ānandamātram avikalpam aviddhavarcaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 3.1]

bhaktyā gṛhītacaraṇaḥ parayā ca teṣāṃ nāpaiṣi nātha hṛdayāmburuhāt svapuṃsām | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 5.2]
tāvad bhayaṃ draviṇadehasuhṛnnimittaṃ śokaḥ spṛhā paribhavo vipulaś ca lobhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 6.1]

kṣuttṛṭtridhātubhir imā muhur ardyamānāḥ śītoṣṇavātavarṣair itaretarāc ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 8.1]
kāmāgninācyutaruṣā ca sudurbhareṇa sampaśyato mana urukrama sīdate me | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 8.2]
yāvat pṛthaktvam idam ātmana indriyārthamāyābalaṃ bhagavato jana īśa paśyet | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 9.1]
tāvan na saṃsṛtir asau pratisaṃkrameta vyarthāpi duḥkhanivahaṃ vahatī kriyārthā | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 9.2]
ahny āpṛtārtakaraṇā niśi niḥśayānā nānāmanorathadhiyā kṣaṇabhagnanidrāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 10.1]
daivāhatārtharacanā ṛṣayo 'pi deva yuṣmatprasaṅgavimukhā iha saṃsaranti | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 10.2]
tvaṃ bhaktiyogaparibhāvitahṛtsaroja āsse śrutekṣitapatho nanu nātha puṃsām | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 11.1]
yadyaddhiyā ta urugāya vibhāvayanti tattadvapuḥ praṇayase sadanugrahāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 11.2]
nātiprasīdati tathopacitopacārair ārādhitaḥ suragaṇair hṛdi baddhakāmaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 12.1]
yat sarvabhūtadayayāsadalabhyayaiko nānājaneṣv avahitaḥ suhṛd antarātmā | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 12.2]
puṃsām ato vividhakarmabhir adhvarādyair dānena cogratapasā paricaryayā ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 13.1]
ārādhanaṃ bhagavatas tava satkriyārtho dharmo 'rpitaḥ karhicin mriyate na yatra | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 13.2]
śaśvat svarūpamahasaiva nipītabhedamohāya bodhadhiṣaṇāya namaḥ parasmai | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 14.1]
viśvodbhavasthitilayeṣu nimittalīlārāsāya te nama idaṃ cakṛmeśvarāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 14.2]
yasyāvatāraguṇakarmaviḍambanāni nāmāni ye 'suvigame vivaśā gṛṇanti | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 15.1]
te 'naikajanmaśamalaṃ sahasaiva hitvā saṃyānty apāvṛtāmṛtaṃ tam ajaṃ prapadye | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 15.2]
yo vā ahaṃ ca giriśaś ca vibhuḥ svayaṃ ca sthityudbhavapralayahetava ātmamūlam | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 16.1]
bhittvā tripād vavṛdha eka uruprarohas tasmai namo bhagavate bhuvanadrumāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 16.2]
loko vikarmanirataḥ kuśale pramattaḥ karmaṇy ayaṃ tvadudite bhavadarcane sve | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 17.1]
yas tāvad asya balavān iha jīvitāśāṃ sadyaś chinatty animiṣāya namo 'stu tasmai | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 17.2]
yasmād bibhemy aham api dviparārdhadhiṣṇyam adhyāsitaḥ sakalalokanamaskṛtaṃ yat | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 18.1]
tepe tapo bahusavo 'varurutsamānas tasmai namo bhagavate 'dhimakhāya tubhyam | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 18.2]
tiryaṅmanuṣyavibudhādiṣu jīvayoniṣv ātmecchayātmakṛtasetuparīpsayā yaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 19.1]
reme nirastaviṣayo 'py avaruddhadehas tasmai namo bhagavate puruṣottamāya | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 19.2]
yo 'vidyayānupahato 'pi daśārdhavṛttyā nidrām uvāha jaṭharīkṛtalokayātraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 20.1]
antarjale 'hikaśipusparśānukūlāṃ bhīmormimālini janasya sukhaṃ vivṛṇvan | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 20.2]
yan nābhipadmabhavanād aham āsam īḍya lokatrayopakaraṇo yadanugraheṇa | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 21.1]

eṣa prapannavarado ramayātmaśaktyā yad yat kariṣyati gṛhītaguṇāvatāraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 23.1]

utthāya viśvavijayāya ca no viṣādaṃ mādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 25.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 26.1]
svasambhavaṃ niśāmyaivaṃ tapovidyāsamādhibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 26.2]
yāvan manovacaḥ stutvā virarāma sa khinnavat | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 26.3]
athābhipretam anvīkṣya brahmaṇo madhusūdanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 27.1]
viṣaṇṇacetasaṃ tena kalpavyatikarāmbhasā | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 27.2]

tan mayāpāditaṃ hy agre yan māṃ prārthayate bhavān | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 29.3]
bhūyas tvaṃ tapa ātiṣṭha vidyāṃ caiva madāśrayām | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 30.1]

svarūpeṇa mayopetaṃ paśyan svārājyam ṛcchati | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 33.2]

nātmāvasīdaty asmiṃs te varṣīyān madanugrahaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 34.2]

yan mano mayi nirbaddhaṃ prajāḥ saṃsṛjato 'pi te | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 35.2]

nālena salile mūlaṃ puṣkarasya vicinvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 9 37.2]

{BhāgPur, 3, 11}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 11 1.1]

maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 1.1]
prājāpatyaṃ tu tat tejaḥ paratejohanaṃ ditiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 1.2]
dadhāra varṣāṇi śataṃ śaṅkamānā surārdanāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 1.3]
loke tenāhatāloke lokapālā hataujasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 2.1]
nyavedayan viśvasṛje dhvāntavyatikaraṃ diśām | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 2.2]
devā ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 3.1]
tama etad vibho vettha saṃvignā yad vayaṃ bhṛśam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 3.2]
na hy avyaktaṃ bhagavataḥ kālenāspṛṣṭavartmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 3.3]
devadeva jagaddhātar lokanāthaśikhāmaṇe | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 4.1]
pareṣām apareṣāṃ tvaṃ bhūtānām asi bhāvavit | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 4.2]

gṛhītaguṇabhedāya namas te 'vyaktayonaye | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 5.2]
ye tvānanyena bhāvena bhāvayanty ātmabhāvanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 6.1]
ātmani protabhuvanaṃ paraṃ sadasadātmakam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 6.2]

labdhayuṣmatprasādānāṃ na kutaścit parābhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 7.2]

haranti balim āyattās tasmai mukhyāya te namaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 8.2]
sa tvaṃ vidhatsva śaṃ bhūmaṃs tamasā luptakarmaṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 9.1]
adabhradayayā dṛṣṭyā āpannān arhasīkṣitum | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 9.2]
eṣa deva diter garbha ojaḥ kāśyapam arpitam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 10.1]
diśas timirayan sarvā vardhate 'gnir ivaidhasi | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 10.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 11.1]
sa prahasya mahābāho bhagavān śabdagocaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 11.2]
pratyācaṣṭātmabhūr devān prīṇan rucirayā girā | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 11.3]
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 12.1]
mānasā me sutā yuṣmatpūrvajāḥ sanakādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 12.2]
cerur vihāyasā lokāl lokeṣu vigataspṛhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 12.3]
ta ekadā bhagavato vaikuṇṭhasyāmalātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 13.1]
yayur vaikuṇṭhanilayaṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 13.2]
vasanti yatra puruṣāḥ sarve vaikuṇṭhamūrtayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 14.1]
ye 'nimittanimittena dharmeṇārādhayan harim | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 14.2]
yatra cādyaḥ pumān āste bhagavān śabdagocaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 15.1]
sattvaṃ viṣṭabhya virajaṃ svānāṃ no mṛḍayan vṛṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 15.2]
yatra naiḥśreyasaṃ nāma vanaṃ kāmadughair drumaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 16.1]
sarvartuśrībhir vibhrājat kaivalyam iva mūrtimat | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 16.2]
vaimānikāḥ salalanāś caritāni śaśvad gāyanti yatra śamalakṣapaṇāni bhartuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 17.1]
antarjale 'nuvikasanmadhumādhavīnāṃ gandhena khaṇḍitadhiyo 'py anilaṃ kṣipantaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 17.2]
pārāvatānyabhṛtasārasacakravākadātyūhahaṃsaśukatittiribarhiṇāṃ yaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 18.1]
kolāhalo viramate 'ciramātram uccair bhṛṅgādhipe harikathām iva gāyamāne | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 18.2]
gandhe 'rcite tulasikābharaṇena tasyā yasmiṃs tapaḥ sumanaso bahu mānayanti | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 19.2]
yat saṃkulaṃ haripadānatimātradṛṣṭair vaiḍūryamārakatahemamayair vimānaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 20.1]
yeṣāṃ bṛhatkaṭitaṭāḥ smitaśobhimukhyaḥ kṛṣṇātmanāṃ na raja ādadhur utsmayādyaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 20.2]
śrī rūpiṇī kvaṇayatī caraṇāravindaṃ līlāmbujena harisadmani muktadoṣā | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 21.1]

vāpīṣu vidrumataṭāsv amalāmṛtāpsu preṣyānvitā nijavane tulasībhir īśam | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 22.1]
abhyarcatī svalakam unnasam īkṣya vaktram uccheṣitaṃ bhagavatety amatāṅga yacchrīḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 22.2]
yan na vrajanty aghabhido racanānuvādāc chṛṇvanti ye 'nyaviṣayāḥ kukathā matighnīḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 23.1]
yās tu śrutā hatabhagair nṛbhir āttasārās tāṃs tān kṣipanty aśaraṇeṣu tamaḥsu hanta | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 23.2]
ye 'bhyarthitām api ca no nṛgatiṃ prapannā jñānaṃ ca tattvaviṣayaṃ sahadharmaṃ yatra | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 24.1]

yac ca vrajanty animiṣām ṛṣabhānuvṛttyā dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīyaśīlāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 25.1]
bhartur mithaḥ suyaśasaḥ kathanānurāgavaiklavyabāṣpakalayā pulakīkṛtāṅgāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 25.2]
tad viśvagurvadhikṛtaṃ bhuvanaikavandyaṃ divyaṃ vicitravibudhāgryavimānaśociḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 26.1]
āpuḥ parāṃ mudam apūrvam upetya yogamāyābalena munayas tad atho vikuṇṭham | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 26.2]
tasminn atītya munayaḥ ṣaḍ asajjamānāḥ kakṣāḥ samānavayasāv atha saptamāyām | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 27.1]
devāv acakṣata gṛhītagadau parārdhyakeyūrakuṇḍalakirīṭaviṭaṅkaveṣau | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 27.2]
mattadvirephavanamālikayā nivītau vinyastayāsitacatuṣṭayabāhumadhye | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 28.1]

dvāry etayor niviviśur miṣator apṛṣṭvā pūrvā yathā puraṭavajrakapāṭikā yāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 29.1]

tān vīkṣya vātaraśanāṃś caturaḥ kumārān vṛddhān daśārdhavayaso viditātmatattvān | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 30.1]

ūcuḥ suhṛttamadidṛkṣitabhaṅga īṣat kāmānujena sahasā ta upaplutākṣāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 31.2]
munaya ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 32.1]

haṃsaśriyor vyajanayoḥ śivavāyulolacchubhrātapatraśaśikesaraśīkarāmbum | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 38.2]

pītāṃśuke pṛthunitambini visphurantyā kāñcyālibhir virutayā vanamālayā ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 40.1]

tasyāravindanayanasya padāravindakiñjalkamiśratulasīmakarandavāyuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 43.1]
