tasmā idaṃ bhagavate nama id vidhema yo 'nātmanāṃ durudayo bhagavān pratītaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 15 50.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 16}
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 1.1]
iti tad gṛṇatāṃ teṣāṃ munīnāṃ yogadharmiṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 1.2]
pratinandya jagādedaṃ vikuṇṭhanilayo vibhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 1.3]
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 2.1]
etau tau pārṣadau mahyaṃ jayo vijaya eva ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 2.2]
kadarthīkṛtya māṃ yad vo bahv akrātām atikramam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 2.3]
yas tv etayor dhṛto daṇḍo bhavadbhir mām anuvrataiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 3.1]
sa evānumato 'smābhir munayo devahelanāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 3.2]
tad vaḥ prasādayāmy adya brahma daivaṃ paraṃ hi me | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 4.1]
tad dhīty ātmakṛtaṃ manye yat svapuṃbhir asatkṛtāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 4.2]
yan nāmāni ca gṛhṇāti loko bhṛtye kṛtāgasi | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 5.1]
so 'sādhuvādas tatkīrtiṃ hanti tvacam ivāmayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 5.2]
yasyāmṛtāmalayaśaḥśravaṇāvagāhaḥ sadyaḥ punāti jagad āśvapacād vikuṇṭhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 6.1]
so 'haṃ bhavadbhya upalabdhasutīrthakīrtiś chindyāṃ svabāhum api vaḥ pratikūlavṛttim | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 6.2]
yatsevayā caraṇapadmapavitrareṇuṃ sadyaḥ kṣatākhilamalaṃ pratilabdhaśīlam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 7.1]
na śrīr viraktam api māṃ vijahāti yasyāḥ prekṣālavārtha itare niyamān vahanti | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 7.2]
nāhaṃ tathādmi yajamānahavir vitāne ścyotadghṛtaplutam adan hutabhuṅmukhena | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 8.1]
yad brāhmaṇasya mukhataś carato 'nughāsaṃ tuṣṭasya mayy avahitair nijakarmapākaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 8.2]
yeṣāṃ bibharmy aham akhaṇḍavikuṇṭhayogamāyāvibhūtir amalāṅghrirajaḥ kirīṭaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 9.1]
viprāṃs tu ko na viṣaheta yadarhaṇāmbhaḥ sadyaḥ punāti sahacandralalāmalokān | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 9.2]
ye me tanūr dvijavarān duhatīr madīyā bhūtāny alabdhaśaraṇāni ca bhedabuddhyā | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 10.1]
drakṣyanty aghakṣatadṛśo hy ahimanyavas tān gṛdhrā ruṣā mama kuṣanty adhidaṇḍanetuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 10.2]
ye brāhmaṇān mayi dhiyā kṣipato 'rcayantas tuṣyaddhṛdaḥ smitasudhokṣitapadmavaktrāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 11.1]
vāṇyānurāgakalayātmajavad gṛṇantaḥ saṃbodhayanty aham ivāham upāhṛtas taiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 11.2]
tan me svabhartur avasāyam alakṣamāṇau yuṣmadvyatikramagatiṃ pratipadya sadyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 12.1]
bhūyo mamāntikam itāṃ tad anugraho me yat kalpatām acirato bhṛtayor vivāsaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 12.2]
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 13.1]
atha tasyośatīṃ devīm ṛṣikulyāṃ sarasvatīm | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 13.2]
nāsvādya manyudaṣṭānāṃ teṣām ātmāpy atṛpyata | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 13.3]
satīṃ vyādāya śṛṇvanto laghvīṃ gurvarthagahvarām | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 14.1]
vigāhyāgādhagambhīrāṃ na vidus taccikīrṣitam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 14.2]
te yogamāyayārabdhapārameṣṭhyamahodayam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 15.1]
procuḥ prāñjalayo viprāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ kṣubhitatvacaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 15.2]
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 16.1]
na vayaṃ bhagavan vidmas tava deva cikīrṣitam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 16.2]
kṛto me 'nugrahaś ceti yad adhyakṣaḥ prabhāṣase | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 16.3]
brahmaṇyasya paraṃ daivaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ kila te prabho | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 17.1]
viprāṇāṃ devadevānāṃ bhagavān ātmadaivatam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 17.2]
tvattaḥ sanātano dharmo rakṣyate tanubhis tava | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 18.1]
dharmasya paramo guhyo nirvikāro bhavān mataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 18.2]
taranti hy añjasā mṛtyuṃ nivṛttā yadanugrahāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 19.1]
yoginaḥ sa bhavān kiṃ svid anugṛhyeta yat paraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 19.2]
yaṃ vai vibhūtir upayāty anuvelam anyair arthārthibhiḥ svaśirasā dhṛtapādareṇuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 20.1]
dhanyārpitāṅghritulasīnavadāmadhāmno lokaṃ madhuvratapater iva kāmayānā | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 20.2]
yas tāṃ viviktacaritair anuvartamānāṃ nātyādriyat paramabhāgavataprasaṅgaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 21.1]
sa tvaṃ dvijānupathapuṇyarajaḥpunītaḥ śrīvatsalakṣma kim agā bhagabhājanas tvam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 21.2]
dharmasya te bhagavatas triyuga tribhiḥ svaiḥ padbhiś carācaram idaṃ dvijadevatārtham | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 22.1]
nūnaṃ bhṛtaṃ tadabhighāti rajas tamaś ca sattvena no varadayā tanuvā nirasya | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 22.2]
na tvaṃ dvijottamakulaṃ yadi hātmagopaṃ goptā vṛṣaḥ svarhaṇena sasūnṛtena | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 23.1]
tarhy eva naṅkṣyati śivas tava deva panthā loko 'grahīṣyad ṛṣabhasya hi tat pramāṇam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 23.2]
tat te 'nabhīṣṭam iva sattvanidher vidhitsoḥ kṣemaṃ janāya nijaśaktibhir uddhṛtāreḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 24.1]
naitāvatā tryadhipater bata viśvabhartus tejaḥ kṣataṃ tv avanatasya sa te vinodaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 24.2]
yaṃ vānayor damam adhīśa bhavān vidhatte vṛttiṃ nu vā tad anumanmahi nirvyalīkam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 25.1]
asmāsu vā ya ucito dhriyatāṃ sa daṇḍo ye 'nāgasau vayam ayuṅkṣmahi kilbiṣeṇa | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 25.2]
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 26.1]
etau suretaragatiṃ pratipadya sadyaḥ saṃrambhasambhṛtasamādhyanubaddhayogau | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 26.2]
bhūyaḥ sakāśam upayāsyata āśu yo vaḥ śāpo mayaiva nimitas tad aveta viprāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 26.3]
brahmovāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 27.1]
atha te munayo dṛṣṭvā nayanānandabhājanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 27.2]
vaikuṇṭhaṃ tadadhiṣṭhānaṃ vikuṇṭhaṃ ca svayamprabham | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 27.3]
bhagavantaṃ parikramya praṇipatyānumānya ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 28.1]
pratijagmuḥ pramuditāḥ śaṃsanto vaiṣṇavīṃ śriyam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 28.2]

brahmatejaḥ samartho 'pi hantuṃ necche mataṃ tu me | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 29.2]
etat puraiva nirdiṣṭaṃ ramayā kruddhayā yadā | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 30.1]
purāpavāritā dvāri viśantī mayy upārate | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 30.2]
mayi saṃrambhayogena nistīrya brahmahelanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 31.1]
pratyeṣyataṃ nikāśaṃ me kālenālpīyasā punaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 31.2]
dvāḥsthāv ādiśya bhagavān vimānaśreṇibhūṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 32.1]
sarvātiśayayā lakṣmyā juṣṭaṃ svaṃ dhiṣṇyam āviśat | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 32.2]
tau tu gīrvāṇaṛṣabhau dustarāddharilokataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 33.1]
hataśriyau brahmaśāpād abhūtāṃ vigatasmayau | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 33.2]
tadā vikuṇṭhadhiṣaṇāt tayor nipatamānayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 34.1]
hāhākāro mahān āsīd vimānāgryeṣu putrakāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 16 34.2]

{BhāgPur, 3, 19}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 19 1.1]
avadhārya viriñcasya nirvyalīkāmṛtaṃ vacaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 19 1.2]

tataḥ sapatnaṃ mukhataś carantam akutobhayam | [BhāgPur, 3, 19 2.1]

sā hatā tena gadayā vihatā bhagavatkarāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 19 3.1]
vighūrṇitāpatad reje tad adbhutam ivābhavat | [BhāgPur, 3, 19 3.2]

{BhāgPur, 3, 20}
śaunaka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 20 1.1]

saṃhatya daivayogena haimam aṇḍam avāsṛjan | [BhāgPur, 3, 20 14.2]

aho rūpam aho dhairyam aho asyā navaṃ vayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 20 32.1]

vitarkayanto bahudhā tāṃ saṃdhyāṃ pramadākṛtim | [BhāgPur, 3, 20 33.1]

nabho dadāti śvasatāṃ padaṃ yanniyamād adaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 29 43.1]

guṇābhimānino devāḥ sargādiṣv asya yadbhayāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 29 44.1]
vartante 'nuyugaṃ yeṣāṃ vaśa etac carācaram | [BhāgPur, 3, 29 44.2]
so 'nanto 'ntakaraḥ kālo 'nādir ādikṛd avyayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 29 45.1]
janaṃ janena janayan mārayan mṛtyunāntakam | [BhāgPur, 3, 29 45.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 30}
kapila uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 1.1]
tasyaitasya jano nūnaṃ nāyaṃ vedoruvikramam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 1.2]
kālyamāno 'pi balino vāyor iva ghanāvaliḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 1.3]
yaṃ yam artham upādatte duḥkhena sukhahetave | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 2.1]
taṃ taṃ dhunoti bhagavān pumān śocati yatkṛte | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 2.2]
yad adhruvasya dehasya sānubandhasya durmatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 3.1]
dhruvāṇi manyate mohād gṛhakṣetravasūni ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 3.2]
jantur vai bhava etasmin yāṃ yāṃ yonim anuvrajet | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 4.1]
tasyāṃ tasyāṃ sa labhate nirvṛtiṃ na virajyate | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 4.2]
narakastho 'pi dehaṃ vai na pumāṃs tyaktum icchati | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 5.1]
nārakyāṃ nirvṛtau satyāṃ devamāyāvimohitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 5.2]
ātmajāyāsutāgārapaśudraviṇabandhuṣu | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 6.1]
nirūḍhamūlahṛdaya ātmānaṃ bahu manyate | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 6.2]
saṃdahyamānasarvāṅga eṣām udvahanādhinā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 7.1]
karoty avirataṃ mūḍho duritāni durāśayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 7.2]
ākṣiptātmendriyaḥ strīṇām asatīnāṃ ca māyayā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 8.1]
raho racitayālāpaiḥ śiśūnāṃ kalabhāṣiṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 8.2]
gṛheṣu kūṭadharmeṣu duḥkhatantreṣv atandritaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 9.1]
kurvan duḥkhapratīkāraṃ sukhavan manyate gṛhī | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 9.2]
arthair āpāditair gurvyā hiṃsayetastataś ca tān | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 10.1]
puṣṇāti yeṣāṃ poṣeṇa śeṣabhug yāty adhaḥ svayam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 10.2]
vārttāyāṃ lupyamānāyām ārabdhāyāṃ punaḥ punaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 11.1]
lobhābhibhūto niḥsattvaḥ parārthe kurute spṛhām | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 11.2]
kuṭumbabharaṇākalpo mandabhāgyo vṛthodyamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 12.1]
śriyā vihīnaḥ kṛpaṇo dhyāyan śvasiti mūḍhadhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 12.2]
evaṃ svabharaṇākalpaṃ tatkalatrādayas tathā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 13.1]
nādriyante yathāpūrvaṃ kīnāśā iva gojaram | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 13.2]
tatrāpy ajātanirvedo bhriyamāṇaḥ svayam bhṛtaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 14.1]
jarayopāttavairūpyo maraṇābhimukho gṛhe | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 14.2]
āste 'vamatyopanyastaṃ gṛhapāla ivāharan | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 15.1]
āmayāvy apradīptāgnir alpāhāro 'lpaceṣṭitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 15.2]
vāyunotkramatottāraḥ kaphasaṃruddhanāḍikaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 16.1]
kāsaśvāsakṛtāyāsaḥ kaṇṭhe ghuraghurāyate | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 16.2]
śayānaḥ pariśocadbhiḥ parivītaḥ svabandhubhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 17.1]
vācyamāno 'pi na brūte kālapāśavaśaṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 17.2]
evaṃ kuṭumbabharaṇe vyāpṛtātmājitendriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 18.1]
mriyate rudatāṃ svānām uruvedanayāstadhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 18.2]
yamadūtau tadā prāptau bhīmau sarabhasekṣaṇau | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 19.1]
sa dṛṣṭvā trastahṛdayaḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ vimuñcati | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 19.2]
yātanādeha āvṛtya pāśair baddhvā gale balāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 20.1]
nayato dīrgham adhvānaṃ daṇḍyaṃ rājabhaṭā yathā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 20.2]
tayor nirbhinnahṛdayas tarjanair jātavepathuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 21.1]
pathi śvabhir bhakṣyamāṇa ārto 'ghaṃ svam anusmaran | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 21.2]
kṣuttṛṭparīto 'rkadavānalānilaiḥ saṃtapyamānaḥ pathi taptavāluke | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 22.1]
kṛcchreṇa pṛṣṭhe kaśayā ca tāḍitaś calaty aśakto 'pi nirāśramodake | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 22.2]
tatra tatra patan śrānto mūrchitaḥ punar utthitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 23.1]
pathā pāpīyasā nītas tarasā yamasādanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 23.2]
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi navatiṃ nava cādhvanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 24.1]
tribhir muhūrtair dvābhyāṃ vā nītaḥ prāpnoti yātanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 24.2]
ādīpanaṃ svagātrāṇāṃ veṣṭayitvolmukādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 25.1]
ātmamāṃsādanaṃ kvāpi svakṛttaṃ parato 'pi vā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 25.2]
jīvataś cāntrābhyuddhāraḥ śvagṛdhrair yamasādane | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 26.1]
sarpavṛścikadaṃśādyair daśadbhiś cātmavaiśasam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 26.2]
kṛntanaṃ cāvayavaśo gajādibhyo bhidāpanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 27.1]
pātanaṃ giriśṛṅgebhyo rodhanaṃ cāmbugartayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 27.2]
yās tāmisrāndhatāmisrā rauravādyāś ca yātanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 28.1]
bhuṅkte naro vā nārī vā mithaḥ saṅgena nirmitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 28.2]
atraiva narakaḥ svarga iti mātaḥ pracakṣate | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 29.1]
yā yātanā vai nārakyas tā ihāpy upalakṣitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 29.2]
evaṃ kuṭumbaṃ bibhrāṇa udaram bhara eva vā | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 30.1]
visṛjyehobhayaṃ pretya bhuṅkte tatphalam īdṛśam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 30.2]
ekaḥ prapadyate dhvāntaṃ hitvedaṃ svakalevaram | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 31.1]
kuśaletarapātheyo bhūtadroheṇa yad bhṛtam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 31.2]
daivenāsāditaṃ tasya śamalaṃ niraye pumān | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 32.1]
bhuṅkte kuṭumbapoṣasya hṛtavitta ivāturaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 32.2]
kevalena hy adharmeṇa kuṭumbabharaṇotsukaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 33.1]
yāti jīvo 'ndhatāmisraṃ caramaṃ tamasaḥ padam | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 33.2]
adhastān naralokasya yāvatīr yātanādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 34.1]
kramaśaḥ samanukramya punar atrāvrajec chuciḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 30 34.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 31}
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 1.1]
karmaṇā daivanetreṇa jantur dehopapattaye | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 1.2]
striyāḥ praviṣṭa udaraṃ puṃso retaḥkaṇāśrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 1.3]
kalalaṃ tv ekarātreṇa pañcarātreṇa budbudam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 2.1]
daśāhena tu karkandhūḥ peśy aṇḍaṃ vā tataḥ param | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 2.2]
māsena tu śiro dvābhyāṃ bāhvaṅghryādyaṅgavigrahaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 3.1]
nakhalomāsthicarmāṇi liṅgacchidrodbhavas tribhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 3.2]
caturbhir dhātavaḥ sapta pañcabhiḥ kṣuttṛḍudbhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 4.1]
ṣaḍbhir jarāyuṇā vītaḥ kukṣau bhrāmyati dakṣiṇe | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 4.2]
mātur jagdhānnapānādyair edhaddhātur asaṃmate | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 5.1]
śete viṇmūtrayor garte sa jantur jantusambhave | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 5.2]
kṛmibhiḥ kṣatasarvāṅgaḥ saukumāryāt pratikṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 6.1]
mūrchām āpnoty urukleśas tatratyaiḥ kṣudhitair muhuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 6.2]
kaṭutīkṣṇoṣṇalavaṇarūkṣāmlādibhir ulbaṇaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 7.1]
mātṛbhuktair upaspṛṣṭaḥ sarvāṅgotthitavedanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 7.2]
ulbena saṃvṛtas tasminn antraiś ca bahir āvṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 8.1]
āste kṛtvā śiraḥ kukṣau bhugnapṛṣṭhaśirodharaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 8.2]
akalpaḥ svāṅgaceṣṭāyāṃ śakunta iva pañjare | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 9.1]
tatra labdhasmṛtir daivāt karma janmaśatodbhavam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 9.2]
smaran dīrgham anucchvāsaṃ śarma kiṃ nāma vindate | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 9.3]
ārabhya saptamān māsāl labdhabodho 'pi vepitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 10.1]
naikatrāste sūtivātair viṣṭhābhūr iva sodaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 10.2]
nāthamāna ṛṣir bhītaḥ saptavadhriḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 11.1]
stuvīta taṃ viklavayā vācā yenodare 'rpitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 11.2]
jantur uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 12.1]
tasyopasannam avituṃ jagad icchayāttanānātanor bhuvi calaccaraṇāravindam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 12.2]
so 'haṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ hy akutobhayaṃ me yenedṛśī gatir adarśy asato 'nurūpā | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 12.3]
yas tv atra baddha iva karmabhir āvṛtātmā bhūtendriyāśayamayīm avalambya māyām | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 13.1]
āste viśuddham avikāram akhaṇḍabodham ātapyamānahṛdaye 'vasitaṃ namāmi | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 13.2]
yaḥ pañcabhūtaracite rahitaḥ śarīre channo 'yathendriyaguṇārthacidātmako 'ham | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 14.1]
tena vikuṇṭhamahimānam ṛṣiṃ tam enaṃ vande paraṃ prakṛtipūruṣayoḥ pumāṃsam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 14.2]
yanmāyayoruguṇakarmanibandhane 'smin sāṃsārike pathi caraṃs tadabhiśrameṇa | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 15.1]
naṣṭasmṛtiḥ punar ayaṃ pravṛṇīta lokaṃ yuktyā kayā mahadanugraham antareṇa | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 15.2]
jñānaṃ yad etad adadhāt katamaḥ sa devas traikālikaṃ sthiracareṣv anuvartitāṃśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 16.1]
taṃ jīvakarmapadavīm anuvartamānās tāpatrayopaśamanāya vayaṃ bhajema | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 16.2]
dehy anyadehavivare jaṭharāgnināsṛgviṇmūtrakūpapatito bhṛśataptadehaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 17.1]
icchann ito vivasituṃ gaṇayan svamāsān nirvāsyate kṛpaṇadhīr bhagavan kadā nu | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 17.2]
yenedṛśīṃ gatim asau daśamāsya īśa saṃgrāhitaḥ purudayena bhavādṛśena | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 18.1]
svenaiva tuṣyatu kṛtena sa dīnanāthaḥ ko nāma tatprati vināñjalim asya kuryāt | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 18.2]
paśyaty ayaṃ dhiṣaṇayā nanu saptavadhriḥ śārīrake damaśarīry aparaḥ svadehe | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 19.1]
yat sṛṣṭayāsaṃ tam ahaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ paśye bahir hṛdi ca caityam iva pratītam | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 19.2]
so 'haṃ vasann api vibho bahuduḥkhavāsaṃ garbhān na nirjigamiṣe bahir andhakūpe | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 20.1]
yatropayātam upasarpati devamāyā mithyā matir yadanu saṃsṛticakram etat | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 20.2]
tasmād ahaṃ vigataviklava uddhariṣya ātmānam āśu tamasaḥ suhṛdātmanaiva | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 21.1]
bhūyo yathā vyasanam etad anekarandhraṃ mā me bhaviṣyad upasāditaviṣṇupādaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 21.2]
kapila uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 22.1]
evaṃ kṛtamatir garbhe daśamāsyaḥ stuvann ṛṣiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 22.2]
sadyaḥ kṣipaty avācīnaṃ prasūtyai sūtimārutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 22.3]
tenāvasṛṣṭaḥ sahasā kṛtvāvāk śira āturaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 23.1]
viniṣkrāmati kṛcchreṇa nirucchvāso hatasmṛtiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 23.2]
patito bhuvy asṛṅmiśraḥ viṣṭhābhūr iva ceṣṭate | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 24.1]
rorūyati gate jñāne viparītāṃ gatiṃ gataḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 24.2]
paracchandaṃ na viduṣā puṣyamāṇo janena saḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 25.1]
anabhipretam āpannaḥ pratyākhyātum anīśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 31 25.2]
{BhāgPur, 3, 32}
kapila uvāca | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 1.1]
atha yo gṛhamedhīyān dharmān evāvasan gṛhe | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 1.2]
kāmam arthaṃ ca dharmān svān dogdhi bhūyaḥ piparti tān | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 1.3]
sa cāpi bhagavaddharmāt kāmamūḍhaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 2.1]
yajate kratubhir devān pitṝṃś ca śraddhayānvitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 2.2]
tacchraddhayākrāntamatiḥ pitṛdevavrataḥ pumān | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 3.1]
gatvā cāndramasaṃ lokaṃ somapāḥ punar eṣyati | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 3.2]
yadā cāhīndraśayyāyāṃ śete 'nantāsano hariḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 4.1]
tadā lokā layaṃ yānti ta ete gṛhamedhinām | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 4.2]
ye svadharmān na duhyanti dhīrāḥ kāmārthahetave | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 5.1]
niḥsaṅgā nyastakarmāṇaḥ praśāntāḥ śuddhacetasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 5.2]
nivṛttidharmaniratā nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 6.1]
svadharmāptena sattvena pariśuddhena cetasā | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 6.2]
sūryadvāreṇa te yānti puruṣaṃ viśvatomukham | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 7.1]
parāvareśaṃ prakṛtim asyotpattyantabhāvanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 7.2]
dviparārdhāvasāne yaḥ pralayo brahmaṇas tu te | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 8.1]
tāvad adhyāsate lokaṃ parasya paracintakāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 8.2]
kṣmāmbho 'nalānilaviyanmana indriyārthabhūtādibhiḥ parivṛtaṃ pratisaṃjihīrṣuḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 9.1]
avyākṛtaṃ viśati yarhi guṇatrayātmā kālaṃ parākhyam anubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 9.2]
evaṃ paretya bhagavantam anupraviṣṭāye yogino jitamarunmanaso virāgāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 10.1]
tenaiva sākam amṛtaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ brahma pradhānam upayānty agatābhimānāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 10.2]
atha taṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛtpadmeṣu kṛtālayam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 11.1]
śrutānubhāvaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja bhāvena bhāmini | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 11.2]
ādyaḥ sthiracarāṇāṃ yo vedagarbhaḥ saharṣibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 12.1]
yogeśvaraiḥ kumārādyaiḥ siddhair yogapravartakaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 12.2]
bhedadṛṣṭyābhimānena niḥsaṅgenāpi karmaṇā | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 13.1]
kartṛtvāt saguṇaṃ brahma puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabham | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 13.2]
sa saṃsṛtya punaḥ kāle kāleneśvaramūrtinā | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 14.1]
jāte guṇavyatikare yathāpūrvaṃ prajāyate | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 14.2]
aiśvaryaṃ pārameṣṭhyaṃ ca te 'pi dharmavinirmitam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 15.1]
niṣevya punar āyānti guṇavyatikare sati | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 15.2]
ye tv ihāsaktamanasaḥ karmasu śraddhayānvitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 16.1]
kurvanty apratiṣiddhāni nityāny api ca kṛtsnaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 16.2]
rajasā kuṇṭhamanasaḥ kāmātmāno 'jitendriyāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 17.1]
pitṝn yajanty anudinaṃ gṛheṣv abhiratāśayāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 17.2]
traivargikās te puruṣā vimukhā harimedhasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 18.1]
kathāyāṃ kathanīyoruvikramasya madhudviṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 18.2]
nūnaṃ daivena vihatā ye cācyutakathāsudhām | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 19.1]
hitvā śṛṇvanty asadgāthāḥ purīṣam iva viḍbhujaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 19.2]
dakṣiṇena pathāryamṇaḥ pitṛlokaṃ vrajanti te | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 20.1]
prajām anu prajāyante śmaśānāntakriyākṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 20.2]
tatas te kṣīṇasukṛtāḥ punar lokam imaṃ sati | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 21.1]
patanti vivaśā devaiḥ sadyo vibhraṃśitodayāḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 21.2]
tasmāt tvaṃ sarvabhāvena bhajasva parameṣṭhinam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 22.1]
tadguṇāśrayayā bhaktyā bhajanīyapadāmbujam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 22.2]
vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ prayojitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 23.1]
janayaty āśu vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ yad brahmadarśanam | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 23.2]
yadāsya cittam artheṣu sameṣv indriyavṛttibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 24.1]
na vigṛhṇāti vaiṣamyaṃ priyam apriyam ity uta | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 24.2]

yenānubudhyate tattvaṃ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 31.2]

dvayor apy eka evārtho bhagavacchabdalakṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 32.2]
yathendriyaiḥ pṛthagdvārair artho bahuguṇāśrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 33.1]
eko nāneyate tadvad bhagavān śāstravartmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 33.2]

ātmendriyajayenāpi saṃnyāsena ca karmaṇām | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 34.2]
yogena vividhāṅgena bhaktiyogena caiva hi | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 35.1]
dharmeṇobhayacihnena yaḥ pravṛttinivṛttimān | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 35.2]
ātmatattvāvabodhena vairāgyeṇa dṛḍhena ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 36.1]
īyate bhagavān ebhiḥ saguṇo nirguṇaḥ svadṛk | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 36.2]

naitat khalāyopadiśen nāvinītāya karhicit | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 39.1]
na stabdhāya na bhinnāya naiva dharmadhvajāya ca | [BhāgPur, 3, 32 39.2]

{BhāgPur, 3, 33}

bhavitāro 'ṅga bhadraṃ te visrapsyanti ca te yaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 1 31.2]

devā ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 1 55.1]
yo māyayā viracitaṃ nijayātmanīdaṃ khe rūpabhedam iva tatpraticakṣaṇāya | [BhāgPur, 4, 1 55.2]
etena dharmasadane ṛṣimūrtinādya prāduścakāra puruṣāya namaḥ parasmai | [BhāgPur, 4, 1 55.3]

tāv imau vai bhagavato harer aṃśāv ihāgatau | [BhāgPur, 4, 1 58.1]

{BhāgPur, 4, 2}
vidura uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 1.1]
bhave śīlavatāṃ śreṣṭhe dakṣo duhitṛvatsalaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 1.2]
vidveṣam akarot kasmād anādṛtyātmajāṃ satīm | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 1.3]
kas taṃ carācaraguruṃ nirvairaṃ śāntavigraham | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 2.1]
ātmārāmaṃ kathaṃ dveṣṭi jagato daivataṃ mahat | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 2.2]
etad ākhyāhi me brahman jāmātuḥ śvaśurasya ca | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 3.1]
vidveṣas tu yataḥ prāṇāṃs tatyaje dustyajān satī | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 3.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 4.1]
purā viśvasṛjāṃ satre sametāḥ paramarṣayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 4.2]
tathāmaragaṇāḥ sarve sānugā munayo 'gnayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 4.3]

bhrājamānaṃ vitimiraṃ kurvantaṃ tan mahat sadaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 5.2]

sadasaspatibhir dakṣo bhagavān sādhu satkṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 7.1]
ajaṃ lokaguruṃ natvā niṣasāda tadājñayā | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 7.2]
prāṅniṣaṇṇaṃ mṛḍaṃ dṛṣṭvā nāmṛṣyat tadanādṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 8.1]
uvāca vāmaṃ cakṣurbhyām abhivīkṣya dahann iva | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 8.2]
śrūyatāṃ brahmarṣayo me sahadevāḥ sahāgnayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 9.1]

ayaṃ tu lokapālānāṃ yaśoghno nirapatrapaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 10.1]
sadbhir ācaritaḥ panthā yena stabdhena dūṣitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 10.2]
eṣa me śiṣyatāṃ prāpto yan me duhitur agrahīt | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 11.1]

pratyutthānābhivādārhe vācāpy akṛta nocitam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 12.2]
luptakriyāyāśucaye mānine bhinnasetave | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 13.1]
anicchann apy adāṃ bālāṃ śūdrāyevośatīṃ giram | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 13.2]
pretāvāseṣu ghoreṣu pretair bhūtagaṇair vṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 14.1]
aṭaty unmattavan nagno vyuptakeśo hasan rudan | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 14.2]
citābhasmakṛtasnānaḥ pretasraṅnrasthibhūṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 15.1]
śivāpadeśo hy aśivo matto mattajanapriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 15.2]
patiḥ pramathanāthānāṃ tamomātrātmakātmanām | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 15.3]
tasmā unmādanāthāya naṣṭaśaucāya durhṛde | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 16.1]
dattā bata mayā sādhvī codite parameṣṭhinā | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 16.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 17.1]
vinindyaivaṃ sa giriśam apratīpam avasthitam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 17.2]

ayaṃ tu devayajana indropendrādibhir bhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 18.1]
saha bhāgaṃ na labhatāṃ devair devagaṇādhamaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 18.2]

tasmād viniṣkramya vivṛddhamanyur jagāma kauravya nijaṃ niketanam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 19.2]

druhyaty ajñaḥ pṛthagdṛṣṭis tattvato vimukho bhavet | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 21.2]

karmatantraṃ vitanute vedavādavipannadhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 22.2]
buddhyā parābhidhyāyinyā vismṛtātmagatiḥ paśuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 23.1]
strīkāmaḥ so 'stv atitarāṃ dakṣo bastamukho 'cirāt | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 23.2]
vidyābuddhir avidyāyāṃ karmamayyām asau jaḍaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 24.1]
saṃsarantviha ye cāmum anu śarvāvamāninam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 24.2]
giraḥ śrutāyāḥ puṣpiṇyā madhugandhena bhūriṇā | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 25.1]
mathnā conmathitātmānaḥ saṃmuhyantu haradviṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 25.2]
sarvabhakṣā dvijā vṛttyai dhṛtavidyātapovratāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 26.1]
vittadehendriyārāmā yācakā vicarantv iha | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 26.2]
tasyaivaṃ vadataḥ śāpaṃ śrutvā dvijakulāya vai | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 27.1]
bhṛguḥ pratyasṛjacchāpaṃ brahmadaṇḍaṃ duratyayam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 27.2]
bhavavratadharā ye ca ye ca tān samanuvratāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 28.1]
pāṣaṇḍinas te bhavantu sacchāstraparipanthinaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 28.2]
naṣṭaśaucā mūḍhadhiyo jaṭābhasmāsthidhāriṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 29.1]
viśantu śivadīkṣāyāṃ yatra daivaṃ surāsavam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 29.2]
brahma ca brāhmaṇāṃś caiva yad yūyaṃ parinindatha | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 30.1]
setuṃ vidhāraṇaṃ puṃsām ataḥ pāṣaṇḍam āśritāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 30.2]
eṣa eva hi lokānāṃ śivaḥ panthāḥ sanātanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 31.1]
yaṃ pūrve cānusaṃtasthur yatpramāṇaṃ janārdanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 31.2]
tad brahma paramaṃ śuddhaṃ satāṃ vartma sanātanam | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 32.1]
vigarhya yāta pāṣaṇḍaṃ daivaṃ vo yatra bhūtarāṭ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 32.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 33.1]
tasyaivaṃ vadataḥ śāpaṃ bhṛgoḥ sa bhagavān bhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 33.2]
niścakrāma tataḥ kiṃcid vimanā iva sānugaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 33.3]
te 'pi viśvasṛjaḥ satraṃ sahasraparivatsarān | [BhāgPur, 4, 2 34.1]

{BhāgPur, 4, 3}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 1.1]
sadā vidviṣator evaṃ kālo vai dhriyamāṇayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 1.2]
jāmātuḥ śvaśurasyāpi sumahān aticakrame | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 1.3]
yadābhiṣikto dakṣas tu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 2.1]
prajāpatīnāṃ sarveṣām ādhipatye smayo 'bhavat | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 2.2]
iṣṭvā sa vājapeyena brahmiṣṭhān abhibhūya ca | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 3.1]
bṛhaspatisavaṃ nāma samārebhe kratūttamam | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 3.2]
tasmin brahmarṣayaḥ sarve devarṣipitṛdevatāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 4.1]
āsan kṛtasvastyayanās tatpatnyaś ca sabhartṛkāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 4.2]
tad upaśrutya nabhasi khecarāṇāṃ prajalpatām | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 5.1]
satī dākṣāyaṇī devī pitṛyajñamahotsavam | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 5.2]
vrajantīḥ sarvato digbhya upadevavarastriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 6.1]

patiṃ bhūtapatiṃ devam autsukyād abhyabhāṣata | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 7.2]
saty uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 8.1]
prajāpates te śvaśurasya sāmprataṃ niryāpito yajñamahotsavaḥ kila | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 8.2]
vayaṃ ca tatrābhisarāma vāma te yady arthitāmī vibudhā vrajanti hi | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 8.3]
tasmin bhaginyo mama bhartṛbhiḥ svakair dhruvaṃ gamiṣyanti suhṛddidṛkṣavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 9.1]
ahaṃ ca tasmin bhavatābhikāmaye sahopanītaṃ paribarham arhitum | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 9.2]
tatra svasṝr me nanu bhartṛsaṃmitā mātṛṣvasṝḥ klinnadhiyaṃ ca mātaram | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 10.1]
drakṣye cirotkaṇṭhamanā maharṣibhir unnīyamānaṃ ca mṛḍādhvaradhvajam | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 10.2]
tvayy etad āścaryam ajātmamāyayā vinirmitaṃ bhāti guṇatrayātmakam | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 11.1]
tathāpy ahaṃ yoṣid atattvavic ca te dīnā didṛkṣe bhava me bhavakṣitim | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 11.2]
paśya prayāntīr abhavānyayoṣito 'py alaṃkṛtāḥ kāntasakhā varūthaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 12.1]
yāsāṃ vrajadbhiḥ śitikaṇṭha maṇḍitaṃ nabho vimānaiḥ kalahaṃsapāṇḍubhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 12.2]
kathaṃ sutāyāḥ pitṛgehakautukaṃ niśamya dehaḥ suravarya neṅgate | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 13.1]
anāhutā apy abhiyanti sauhṛdaṃ bhartur guror dehakṛtaś ca ketanam | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 13.2]
tan me prasīdedam amartya vāñchitaṃ kartuṃ bhavān kāruṇiko batārhati | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 14.1]
tvayātmano 'rdhe 'ham adabhracakṣuṣā nirūpitā mānugṛhāṇa yācitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 14.2]
ṛṣir uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 15.1]
evaṃ giritraḥ priyayābhibhāṣitaḥ pratyabhyadhatta prahasan suhṛtpriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 15.2]
saṃsmārito marmabhidaḥ kuvāgiṣūn yān āha ko viśvasṛjāṃ samakṣataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 15.3]
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 16.1]
tvayoditaṃ śobhanam eva śobhane anāhutā apy abhiyanti bandhuṣu | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 16.2]
te yady anutpāditadoṣadṛṣṭayo balīyasānātmyamadena manyunā | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 16.3]
vidyātapovittavapurvayaḥkulaiḥ satāṃ guṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir asattametaraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 17.1]
smṛtau hatāyāṃ bhṛtamānadurdṛśaḥ stabdhā na paśyanti hi dhāma bhūyasām | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 17.2]
naitādṛśānāṃ svajanavyapekṣayā gṛhān pratīyād anavasthitātmanām | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 18.1]
ye 'bhyāgatān vakradhiyābhicakṣate āropitabhrūbhir amarṣaṇākṣibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 18.2]
tathāribhir na vyathate śilīmukhaiḥ śete 'rditāṅgo hṛdayena dūyatā | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 19.1]
svānāṃ yathā vakradhiyāṃ duruktibhir divāniśaṃ tapyati marmatāḍitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 19.2]
vyaktaṃ tvam utkṛṣṭagateḥ prajāpateḥ priyātmajānām asi subhru me matā | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 20.1]
tathāpi mānaṃ na pituḥ prapatsyase madāśrayāt kaḥ paritapyate yataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 20.2]
pāpacyamānena hṛdāturendriyaḥ samṛddhibhiḥ pūruṣabuddhisākṣiṇām | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 21.1]
akalpa eṣām adhiroḍhum añjasā paraṃ padaṃ dveṣṭi yathāsurā harim | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 21.2]
pratyudgamapraśrayaṇābhivādanaṃ vidhīyate sādhu mithaḥ sumadhyame | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 22.1]
prājñaiḥ parasmai puruṣāya cetasā guhāśayāyaiva na dehamānine | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 22.2]
sattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ vasudevaśabditaṃ yad īyate tatra pumān apāvṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 23.1]
sattve ca tasmin bhagavān vāsudevo hy adhokṣajo me namasā vidhīyate | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 23.2]
tat te nirīkṣyo na pitāpi dehakṛd dakṣo mama dviṭ tadanuvratāś ca ye | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 24.1]
yo viśvasṛgyajñagataṃ varoru mām anāgasaṃ durvacasākarot tiraḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 24.2]
yadi vrajiṣyasy atihāya madvaco bhadraṃ bhavatyā na tato bhaviṣyati | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 25.1]
saṃbhāvitasya svajanāt parābhavo yadā sa sadyo maraṇāya kalpate | [BhāgPur, 4, 3 25.2]
{BhāgPur, 4, 4}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 1.1]
etāvad uktvā virarāma śaṅkaraḥ patnyaṅganāśaṃ hy ubhayatra cintayan | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 1.2]
suhṛddidṛkṣuḥ pariśaṅkitā bhavān niṣkrāmatī nirviśatī dvidhāsa sā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 1.3]
suhṛddidṛkṣāpratighātadurmanāḥ snehād rudaty aśrukalātivihvalā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 2.1]
bhavaṃ bhavāny apratipūruṣaṃ ruṣā pradhakṣyatīvaikṣata jātavepathuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 2.2]
tato viniḥśvasya satī vihāya taṃ śokena roṣeṇa ca dūyatā hṛdā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 3.1]
pitror agāt straiṇavimūḍhadhīr gṛhān premṇātmano yo 'rdham adāt satāṃ priyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 3.2]
tām anvagacchan drutavikramāṃ satīm ekāṃ trinetrānucarāḥ sahasraśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 4.1]
sapārṣadayakṣā maṇimanmadādayaḥ purovṛṣendrās tarasā gatavyathāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 4.2]
tāṃ sārikākandukadarpaṇāmbujaśvetātapatravyajanasragādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 5.1]
gītāyanair dundubhiśaṅkhaveṇubhir vṛṣendram āropya viṭaṅkitā yayuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 5.2]
ābrahmaghoṣorjitayajñavaiśasaṃ viprarṣijuṣṭaṃ vibudhaiś ca sarvaśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 6.1]
mṛddārvayaḥkāñcanadarbhacarmabhir nisṛṣṭabhāṇḍaṃ yajanaṃ samāviśat | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 6.2]
tām āgatāṃ tatra na kaścanādriyad vimānitāṃ yajñakṛto bhayājjanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 7.1]
ṛte svasṝr vai jananīṃ ca sādarāḥ premāśrukaṇṭhyaḥ pariṣasvajur mudā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 7.2]
saudaryasampraśnasamarthavārtayā mātrā ca mātṛṣvasṛbhiś ca sādaram | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 8.1]
dattāṃ saparyāṃ varam āsanaṃ ca sā nādatta pitrāpratinanditā satī | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 8.2]
arudrabhāgaṃ tam avekṣya cādhvaraṃ pitrā ca deve kṛtahelanaṃ vibhau | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 9.1]
anādṛtā yajñasadasy adhīśvarī cukopa lokān iva dhakṣyatī ruṣā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 9.2]
jagarha sāmarṣavipannayā girā śivadviṣaṃ dhūmapathaśramasmayam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 10.1]
svatejasā bhūtagaṇān samutthitān nigṛhya devī jagato 'bhiśṛṇvataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 10.2]
devy uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 11.1]
na yasya loke 'sty atiśāyanaḥ priyas tathāpriyo dehabhṛtāṃ priyātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 11.2]
tasmin samastātmani muktavairake ṛte bhavantaṃ katamaḥ pratīpayet | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 11.3]
doṣān pareṣāṃ hi guṇeṣu sādhavo gṛhṇanti kecin na bhavādṛśo dvija | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 12.1]
guṇāṃś ca phalgūn bahulīkariṣṇavo mahattamās teṣv avidad bhavān agham | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 12.2]
nāścaryam etad yad asatsu sarvadā mahadvinindā kuṇapātmavādiṣu | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 13.1]
serṣyaṃ mahāpūruṣapādapāṃsubhir nirastatejaḥsu tad eva śobhanam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 13.2]
yad dvyakṣaraṃ nāma gireritaṃ nṛṇāṃ sakṛt prasaṅgād agham āśu hanti tat | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 14.1]
pavitrakīrtiṃ tam alaṅghyaśāsanaṃ bhavān aho dveṣṭi śivaṃ śivetaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 14.2]
yatpādapadmaṃ mahatāṃ mano'libhir niṣevitaṃ brahmarasāsavārthibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 15.1]
lokasya yad varṣati cāśiṣo 'rthinas tasmai bhavān druhyati viśvabandhave | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 15.2]
kiṃvā śivākhyam aśivaṃ na vidus tvad anye brahmādayas tam avakīrya jaṭāḥ śmaśāne | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 16.1]
tanmālyabhasmanṛkapāly avasat piśācair ye mūrdhabhir dadhati taccaraṇāvasṛṣṭam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 16.2]
karṇau pidhāya nirayād yad akalpa īśe dharmāvitary asṛṇibhir nṛbhir asyamāne | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 17.1]
chindyāt prasahya ruśatīm asatīṃ prabhuś cejjihvām asūn api tato visṛjet sa dharmaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 17.2]
atas tavotpannam idaṃ kalevaraṃ na dhārayiṣye śitikaṇṭhagarhiṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 18.1]
jagdhasya mohāddhi viśuddhim andhaso jugupsitasyoddharaṇaṃ pracakṣate | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 18.2]
na vedavādān anuvartate matiḥ sva eva loke ramato mahāmuneḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 19.1]
yathā gatir devamanuṣyayoḥ pṛthak sva eva dharme na paraṃ kṣipet sthitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 19.2]
karma pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttam apy ṛtaṃ vede vivicyobhayaliṅgam āśritam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 20.1]
virodhi tad yaugapadaikakartari dvayaṃ tathā brahmaṇi karma narcchati | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 20.2]
mā vaḥ padavyaḥ pitar asmadāsthitā yā yajñaśālāsu na dhūmavartmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 21.1]
tadannatṛptair asuhṛdbhir īḍitā avyaktaliṅgā avadhūtasevitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 21.2]
naitena dehena hare kṛtāgaso dehodbhavenālam alaṃ kujanmanā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 22.1]
vrīḍā mamābhūt kujanaprasaṅgatas tajjanma dhig yo mahatām avadyakṛt | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 22.2]
gotraṃ tvadīyaṃ bhagavān vṛṣadhvajo dākṣāyaṇīty āha yadā sudurmanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 23.1]
vyapetanarmasmitam āśu tadāhaṃ vyutsrakṣya etat kuṇapaṃ tvadaṅgajam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 23.2]
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 24.1]
ity adhvare dakṣam anūdya śatruhan kṣitāv udīcīṃ niṣasāda śāntavāk | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 24.2]
spṛṣṭvā jalaṃ pītadukūlasaṃvṛtā nimīlya dṛgyogapathaṃ samāviśat | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 24.3]
kṛtvā samānāv anilau jitāsanā sodānam utthāpya ca nābhicakrataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 25.1]
śanair hṛdi sthāpya dhiyorasi sthitaṃ kaṇṭhād bhruvor madhyam aninditānayat | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 25.2]
evaṃ svadehaṃ mahatāṃ mahīyasā muhuḥ samāropitam aṅkam ādarāt | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 26.1]
jihāsatī dakṣaruṣā manasvinī dadhāra gātreṣv anilāgnidhāraṇām | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 26.2]
tataḥ svabhartuś caraṇāmbujāsavaṃ jagadguroś cintayatī na cāparam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 27.1]
dadarśa deho hatakalmaṣaḥ satī sadyaḥ prajajvāla samādhijāgninā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 27.2]
tat paśyatāṃ khe bhuvi cādbhutaṃ mahaddhā heti vādaḥ sumahān ajāyata | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 28.1]
hanta priyā daivatamasya devī jahāv asūn kena satī prakopitā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 28.2]
aho anātmyaṃ mahad asya paśyata prajāpater yasya carācaraṃ prajāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 29.1]
jahāv asūn yadvimatātmajā satī manasvinī mānam abhīkṣṇam arhati | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 29.2]
so 'yaṃ durmarṣahṛdayo brahmadhruk ca loke 'pakīrtiṃ mahatīm avāpsyati | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 30.1]
yadaṅgajāṃ svāṃ puruṣadviḍ udyatāṃ na pratyaṣedhan mṛtaye 'parādhataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 30.2]
vadaty evaṃ jane satyā dṛṣṭvāsutyāgam adbhutam | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 31.1]
dakṣaṃ tatpārṣadā hantum udatiṣṭhann udāyudhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 31.2]
teṣām āpatatāṃ vegaṃ niśāmya bhagavān bhṛguḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 32.1]
yajñaghnaghnena yajuṣā dakṣiṇāgnau juhāva ha | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 32.2]
adhvaryuṇā hūyamāne devā utpetur ojasā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 33.1]
ṛbhavo nāma tapasā somaṃ prāptāḥ sahasraśaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 33.2]
tair alātāyudhaiḥ sarve pramathāḥ sahaguhyakāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 34.1]
hanyamānā diśo bhejur uśadbhir brahmatejasā | [BhāgPur, 4, 4 34.2]
{BhāgPur, 4, 5}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 1.1]
bhavo bhavānyā nidhanaṃ prajāpater asatkṛtāyā avagamya nāradāt | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 1.2]
svapārṣadasainyaṃ ca tadadhvararbhubhir vidrāvitaṃ krodham apāram ādadhe | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 1.3]
kruddhaḥ sudaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭaḥ sa dhūrjaṭir jaṭāṃ taḍidvahnisaṭograrociṣam | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 2.1]
utkṛtya rudraḥ sahasotthito hasan gambhīranādo visasarja tāṃ bhuvi | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 2.2]
tato 'tikāyas tanuvā spṛśan divaṃ sahasrabāhur ghanaruk trisūryadṛk | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 3.1]
karāladaṃṣṭro jvaladagnimūrdhajaḥ kapālamālī vividhodyatāyudhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 3.2]
taṃ kiṃ karomīti gṛṇantam āha baddhāñjaliṃ bhagavān bhūtanāthaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 4.1]
dakṣaṃ sayajñaṃ jahi madbhaṭānāṃ tvam agraṇī rudra bhaṭāṃśako me | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 4.2]
ājñapta evaṃ kupitena manyunā sa devadevaṃ paricakrame vibhum | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 5.1]
mene tadātmānam asaṅgaraṃhasā mahīyasāṃ tāta sahaḥ sahiṣṇum | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 5.2]
anvīyamānaḥ sa tu rudrapārṣadair bhṛśaṃ nadadbhir vyanadat subhairavam | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 6.1]
udyamya śūlaṃ jagadantakāntakaṃ samprādravad ghoṣaṇabhūṣaṇāṅghriḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 6.2]
athartvijo yajamānaḥ sadasyāḥ kakubhyudīcyāṃ prasamīkṣya reṇum | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 7.1]
tamaḥ kimetatkuta etadrajo 'bhūditi dvijā dvijapatnyaśca dadhyuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 7.2]
vātā na vānti na hi santi dasyavaḥ prācīnabarhir jīvati hogradaṇḍaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 8.1]
gāvo na kālyanta idaṃ kuto rajo loko 'dhunā kiṃ pralayāya kalpate | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 8.2]
prasūtimiśrāḥ striya udvignacittā ūcur vipāko vṛjinasyaiva tasya | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 9.1]
yat paśyantīnāṃ duhitṝṇāṃ prajeśaḥ sutāṃ satīm avadadhyāvanāgām | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 9.2]
yastvantakāle vyuptajaṭākalāpaḥ svaśūlasūcyarpitadiggajendraḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 10.1]
vitatya nṛtyatyuditāstradordhvajān uccāṭṭahāsastanayitnubhinnadik | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 10.2]
amarṣayitvā tam asahyatejasaṃ manyuplutaṃ durnirīkṣyaṃ bhrukuṭyā | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 11.1]
karāladaṃṣṭrābhir udastabhāgaṇaṃ syāt svasti kiṃ kopayato vidhātuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 11.2]
bahv evam udvignadṛśocyamāne janena dakṣasya muhur mahātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 12.1]
utpetur utpātatamāḥ sahasraśo bhayāvahā divi bhūmau ca paryak | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 12.2]
tāvat sa rudrānucarair mahāmakho nānāyudhair vāmanakair udāyudhaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 13.1]
piṅgaiḥ piśaṅgair makarodarānanaiḥ paryādravadbhir vidurānvarudhyata | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 13.2]
kecid babhañjuḥ prāgvaṃśaṃ patnīśālāṃ tathāpare | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 14.1]
sada āgnīdhraśālāṃ ca tadvihāraṃ mahānasam | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 14.2]
rurujur yajñapātrāṇi tathaike 'gnīn anāśayan | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 15.1]
kuṇḍeṣv amūtrayan kecid bibhidur vedimekhalāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 15.2]
abādhanta munīn anye eke patnīr atarjayan | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 16.1]
apare jagṛhur devān pratyāsannān palāyitān | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 16.2]
bhṛguṃ babandha maṇimān vīrabhadraḥ prajāpatim | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 17.1]
caṇḍeśaḥ pūṣaṇaṃ devaṃ bhagaṃ nandīśvaro 'grahīt | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 17.2]
sarva evartvijo dṛṣṭvā sadasyāḥ sadivaukasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 18.1]
tair ardyamānāḥ subhṛśaṃ grāvabhir naikadhādravan | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 18.2]
juhvataḥ sruvahastasya śmaśrūṇi bhagavān bhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 19.1]
bhṛgor luluñce sadasi yo 'hasacchmaśru darśayan | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 19.2]
bhagasya netre bhagavān pātitasya ruṣā bhuvi | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 20.1]
ujjahāra sadastho 'kṣṇā yaḥ śapantam asūsucat | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 20.2]
pūṣṇo hy apātayad dantān kāliṅgasya yathā balaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 21.1]
śapyamāne garimaṇi yo 'hasad darśayan dataḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 21.2]
ākramyorasi dakṣasya śitadhāreṇa hetinā | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 22.1]
chindann api tad uddhartuṃ nāśaknot tryambakas tadā | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 22.2]
śastrair astrānvitair evam anirbhinnatvacaṃ haraḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 23.1]
vismayaṃ param āpanno dadhyau paśupatiś ciram | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 23.2]
dṛṣṭvā saṃjñapanaṃ yogaṃ paśūnāṃ sa patir makhe | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 24.1]
yajamānapaśoḥ kasya kāyāt tenāharacchiraḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 24.2]
sādhuvādas tadā teṣāṃ karma tat tasya paśyatām | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 25.1]
bhūtapretapiśācānāṃ anyeṣāṃ tadviparyayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 25.2]
juhāvaitacchirastasmin dakṣiṇāgnāv amarṣitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 26.1]
taddevayajanaṃ dagdhvā prātiṣṭhad guhyakālayam | [BhāgPur, 4, 5 26.2]
{BhāgPur, 4, 6}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 1.1]
atha devagaṇāḥ sarve rudrānīkaiḥ parājitāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 1.2]
śūlapaṭṭiśanistriṃśagadāparighamudgaraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 1.3]
saṃchinnabhinnasarvāṅgāḥ sartviksabhyā bhayākulāḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 2.1]
svayambhuve namaskṛtya kārtsnyenaitan nyavedayan | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 2.2]
upalabhya puraivaitad bhagavān abjasaṃbhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 3.1]
nārāyaṇaś ca viśvātmā na kasyādhvaram īyatuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 3.2]
tad ākarṇya vibhuḥ prāha tejīyasi kṛtāgasi | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 4.1]
kṣemāya tatra sā bhūyān na prāyeṇa bubhūṣatām | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 4.2]
athāpi yūyaṃ kṛtakilbiṣā bhavaṃ ye barhiṣo bhāgabhājaṃ parāduḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 5.1]
prasādayadhvaṃ pariśuddhacetasā kṣipraprasādaṃ pragṛhītāṅghripadmam | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 5.2]
āśāsānā jīvitam adhvarasya lokaḥ sapālaḥ kupite na yasmin | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 6.1]
tam āśu devaṃ priyayā vihīnaṃ kṣamāpayadhvaṃ hṛdi viddhaṃ duruktaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 6.2]
nāhaṃ na yajño na ca yūyam anye ye dehabhājo munayaś ca tattvam | [BhāgPur, 4, 6 7.1]

maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 9 1.1]

{BhāgPur, 4, 14}
maitreya uvāca | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 1.1]

sāntvito yadi no vācaṃ na grahīṣyatyadharmakṛt | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 12.2]
lokadhikkārasaṃdagdhaṃ dahiṣyāmaḥ svatejasā | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 13.1]
evamadhyavasāyainaṃ munayo gūḍhamanyavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 13.2]
upavrajyābruvanvenaṃ sāntvayitvā ca sāmabhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 13.3]
munaya ūcuḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 14.1]
nṛpavarya nibodhaitadyatte vijñāpayāma bhoḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 14.2]
āyuḥśrībalakīrtīnāṃ tava tāta vivardhanam | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 14.3]
dharma ācaritaḥ puṃsāṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyabuddhibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 15.1]
lokānviśokānvitaratyathānantyamasaṅginām | [BhāgPur, 4, 14 15.2]

devakyā garbhasambhūtaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca svavadhaṃ prati | [BhāgPur, 10, 1 65.2]
devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca nigṛhya nigaḍairgṛhe | [BhāgPur, 10, 1 66.1]
jātaṃ jātamahanputraṃ tayorajanaśaṅkayā | [BhāgPur, 10, 1 66.2]

ghnanti hyasutṛpo lubdhā rājānaḥ prāyaśo bhuvi | [BhāgPur, 10, 1 67.2]
ātmānamiha saṃjātaṃ jānanprāgviṣṇunā hatam | [BhāgPur, 10, 1 68.1]

anyaiścāsurabhūpālairbāṇabhaumādibhiryutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 2.1]

eke tamanurundhānā jñātayaḥ paryupāsate | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 4.1]
hateṣu ṣaṭsu bāleṣu devakyā augraseninā | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 4.2]

bhagavānapi viśvātmā viditvā kaṃsajaṃ bhayam | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 6.1]
yadūnāṃ nijanāthānāṃ yogamāyāṃ samādiśat | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 6.2]
gaccha devi vrajaṃ bhadre gopagobhiralaṃkṛtam | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 7.1]

anyāśca kaṃsasaṃvignā vivareṣu vasanti hi | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 7.3]
devakyā jaṭhare garbhaṃ śeṣākhyaṃ dhāma māmakam | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 8.1]
tatsaṃnikṛṣya rohiṇyā udare saṃniveśaya | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 8.2]
athāhamaṃśabhāgena devakyāḥ putratāṃ śubhe | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 9.1]

arciṣyanti manuṣyāstvāṃ sarvakāmavareśvarīm | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 10.1]

nāmadheyāni kurvanti sthānāni ca narā bhuvi | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 11.1]
durgeti bhadrakālīti vijayā vaiṣṇavīti ca | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 11.2]
kumudā caṇḍikā kṛṣṇā mādhavī kanyaketi ca | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 12.1]
māyā nārāyaṇīśānī śāradetyambiketi ca | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 12.2]
garbhasaṃkarṣaṇāttaṃ vai prāhuḥ saṅkarṣaṇaṃ bhuvi | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 13.1]
rāmeti lokaramaṇādbalabhadraṃ balocchrayāt | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 13.2]
saṃdiṣṭaivaṃ bhagavatā tathetyomiti tadvacaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 14.1]
pratigṛhya parikramya gāṃ gatā tattathākarot | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 14.2]
garbhe praṇīte devakyā rohiṇīṃ yoganidrayā | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 15.1]
aho visraṃsito garbha iti paurā vicukruśuḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 15.2]
bhagavānapi viśvātmā bhaktānāmabhayaṅkaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 16.1]
āviveśāṃśabhāgena mana ānakadundubheḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 16.2]

durāsado 'tidurdharṣo bhūtānāṃ saṃbabhūva ha | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 17.2]

bhojendragehe 'gniśikheva ruddhā sarasvatī jñānakhale yathā satī | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 19.2]
tāṃ vīkṣya kaṃsaḥ prabhayājitāntarāṃ virocayantīṃ bhavanaṃ śucismitām | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 20.1]

kimadya tasminkaraṇīyamāśu me yadarthatantro na vihanti vikramam | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 21.1]

sa eṣa jīvankhalu saṃpareto varteta yo 'tyantanṛśaṃsitena | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 22.1]

āste pratīkṣaṃstajjanma harervairānubandhakṛt | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 23.2]

cintayāno hṛṣīkeśamapaśyattanmayaṃ jagat | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 24.2]
brahmā bhavaśca tatraitya munibhirnāradādibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 25.1]
devaiḥ sānucaraiḥ sākaṃ gīrbhirvṛṣaṇam aiḍayan | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 25.2]

ekāyano 'sau dviphalastrimūlaścatūrasaḥ pañcavidhaḥ ṣaḍātmā | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 27.1]

tvameka evāsya sataḥ prasūtistvaṃ sannidhānaṃ tvamanugrahaśca | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 28.1]

bibharṣi rūpāṇyavabodha ātmā kṣemāya lokasya carācarasya | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 29.1]
sattvopapannāni sukhāvahāni satāmabhadrāṇi muhuḥ khalānām | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 29.2]
tvayyambujākṣākhilasattvadhāmni samādhināveśitacetasaike | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 30.1]
tvatpādapotena mahatkṛtena kurvanti govatsapadaṃ bhavābdhim | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 30.2]
svayaṃ samuttīrya sudustaraṃ dyuman bhavārṇavaṃ bhīmamadabhrasauhṛdāḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 31.1]

tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacidbhraśyanti mārgāttvayi baddhasauhṛdāḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 33.1]
tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayā vināyakānīkapamūrdhasu prabho | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 33.2]

vedakriyāyogatapaḥsamādhibhistavārhaṇaṃ yena janaḥ samīhate | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 34.2]

guṇaprakāśairanumīyate bhavānprakāśate yasya ca yena vā guṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 35.2]

na te 'bhavasyeśa bhavasya kāraṇaṃ vinā vinodaṃ bata tarkayāmahe | [BhāgPur, 10, 2 39.1]

śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 1.1]
atha sarvaguṇopetaḥ kālaḥ paramaśobhanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 1.2]
yarhyevājanajanmarkṣaṃ śāntarkṣagrahatārakam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 1.3]
diśaḥ prasedurgaganaṃ nirmaloḍugaṇodayam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 2.1]

dvijālikulasannādastavakā vanarājayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 3.2]
vavau vāyuḥ sukhasparśaḥ puṇyagandhavahaḥ śuciḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 4.1]

manāṃsyāsanprasannāni sādhūnāmasuradruhām | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 5.1]

niśīthe tamaudbhūte jāyamāne janārdane | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 8.1]
devakyāṃ devarūpiṇyāṃ viṣṇuḥ sarvaguhāśayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 8.2]
āvirāsīdyathā prācyāṃ diśīnduriva puṣkalaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 8.3]
tamadbhutaṃ bālakamambujekṣaṇaṃ caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhagadādyudāyudham | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 9.1]
śrīvatsalakṣmaṃ galaśobhikaustubhaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sāndrapayodasaubhagam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 9.2]
mahārhavaidūryakirīṭakuṇḍalatviṣā pariṣvaktasahasrakuntalam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 10.1]

kṛṣṇāvatārotsavasambhramo 'spṛśanmudā dvijebhyo 'yutamāpluto gavām | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 11.2]
athainamastaudavadhārya pūruṣaṃ paraṃ natāṅgaḥ kṛtadhīḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 12.1]
svarociṣā bhārata sūtikāgṛhaṃ virocayantaṃ gatabhīḥ prabhāvavit | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 12.2]
śrīvasudeva uvāca | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 13.1]
vidito 'si bhavānsākṣātpuruṣaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 13.2]
kevalānubhavānandasvarūpaḥ sarvabuddhidṛk | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 13.3]
sa eva svaprakṛtyedaṃ sṛṣṭvāgre triguṇātmakam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 14.1]
tadanu tvaṃ hyapraviṣṭaḥ praviṣṭa iva bhāvyase | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 14.2]
yatheme 'vikṛtā bhāvāstathā te vikṛtaiḥ saha | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 15.1]
nānāvīryāḥ pṛthagbhūtā virājaṃ janayanti hi | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 15.2]
saṃnipatya samutpādya dṛśyante 'nugatā iva | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 16.1]
prāgeva vidyamānatvānna teṣāmiha sambhavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 16.2]

ya ātmano dṛśyaguṇeṣu sanniti vyavasyate svavyatirekato 'budhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 18.1]
vinānuvādaṃ na ca tanmanīṣitaṃ samyagyatastyaktam upādadat pumān | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 18.2]
tvatto 'sya janmasthitisaṃyamānvibho vadantyanīhādaguṇādavikriyāt | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 19.1]
tvayīśvare brahmaṇi no virudhyate tvadāśrayatvādupacaryate guṇaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 19.2]
sa tvaṃ trilokasthitaye svamāyayā bibharṣi śuklaṃ khalu varṇamātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 20.1]
sargāya raktaṃ rajasopabṛṃhitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca varṇaṃ tamasā janātyaye | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 20.2]
tvamasya lokasya vibho rirakṣiṣurgṛhe 'vatīrṇo 'si mamākhileśvara | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 21.1]
rājanyasaṃjñāsurakoṭiyūthapair nirvyūhyamānā nihaniṣyase camūḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 21.2]

śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 23.1]
athainamātmajaṃ vīkṣya mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 23.2]
devakī tamupādhāvatkaṃsādbhītā suvismitā | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 23.3]
śrīdevakyuvāca | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 24.1]

naṣṭe loke dviparārdhāvasāne mahābhūteṣvādibhūtaṃ gateṣu | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 25.1]
vyakte 'vyaktaṃ kālavegena yāte bhavānekaḥ śiṣyate 'śeṣasaṃjñaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 25.2]
yo 'yaṃ kālastasya te 'vyaktabandho ceṣṭāmāhuśceṣṭate yena viśvam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 26.1]
nimeṣādirvatsarānto mahīyāṃstaṃ tveśānaṃ kṣemadhāma prapadye | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 26.2]
martyo mṛtyuvyālabhītaḥ palāyanlokānsarvānnirbhayaṃ nādhyagacchat | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 27.1]
tvatpādābjaṃ prāpya yadṛcchayādya susthaḥ śete mṛtyurasmādapaiti | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 27.2]
sa tvaṃ ghorādugrasenātmajānnastrāhi trastān bhṛtyavitrāsahāsi | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 28.1]
rūpaṃ cedaṃ pauruṣaṃ dhyānadhiṣṇyaṃ mā pratyakṣaṃ māṃsadṛśāṃ kṛṣīṣṭhāḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 28.2]
janma te mayyasau pāpo mā vidyānmadhusūdana | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 29.1]
samudvije bhavaddhetoḥ kaṃsādahamadhīradhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 29.2]
upasaṃhara viśvātmannado rūpamalaukikam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 30.1]
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaśriyā juṣṭaṃ caturbhujam | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 30.2]
viśvaṃ yadetatsvatanau niśānte yathāvakāśaṃ puruṣaḥ paro bhavān | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 31.1]
bibharti so 'yaṃ mama garbhago 'bhūdaho nṛlokasya viḍambanaṃ hi tat | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 31.2]
śrībhagavānuvāca | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 32.1]
tvameva pūrvasarge 'bhūḥ pṛśniḥ svāyambhuve sati | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 32.2]
tadāyaṃ sutapā nāma prajāpatirakalmaṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 10, 3 32.3]

śrīśuka uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 1.1]

syān nas tavāṅghrir aśubhāśayadhūmaketuḥ kṣemāya yo munibhir ārdrahṛdohyamānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 10.1]
yaḥ sātvataiḥ samavibhūtaya ātmavadbhir vyūhe 'rcitaḥ savanaśaḥ svaratikramāya | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 10.2]

paryuṣṭayā tava vibho vanamālayeyaṃ saṃspardhinī bhagavatī pratipatnīvac chrīḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 12.1]
yaḥ supraṇītam amuyārhaṇam ādadan no bhūyāt sadāṅghrir aśubhāśayadhūmaketuḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 12.2]
ketus trivikramayutas tripatatpatāko yas te bhayābhayakaro 'suradevacamvoḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 6 13.1]

{BhāgPur, 11, 8}
śrībrāhmaṇa uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 1.1]
sukham aindriyakaṃ rājan svarge naraka eva ca | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 1.2]
dehināṃ yad yathā duḥkhaṃ tasmān neccheta tadbudhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 1.3]
grāsaṃ sumṛṣṭaṃ virasaṃ mahāntaṃ stokam eva vā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 2.1]
yadṛcchayaivāpatitaṃ grased ājagaro 'kriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 2.2]
śayītāhāni bhūrīṇi nirāhāro 'nupakramaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 3.1]
yadi nopanayed grāso mahāhir iva diṣṭabhuk | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 3.2]
ojaḥsahobalayutaṃ bibhrad deham akarmakam | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 4.1]
śayāno vītanidraś ca nehetendriyavān api | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 4.2]
muniḥ prasannagambhīro durvigāhyo duratyayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 5.1]
anantapāro hy akṣobhyaḥ stimitoda ivārṇavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 5.2]
samṛddhakāmo hīno vā nārāyaṇaparo muniḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 6.1]
notsarpeta na śuṣyeta saridbhir iva sāgaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 6.2]
dṛṣṭvā striyaṃ devamāyāṃ tadbhāvair ajitendriyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 7.1]
pralobhitaḥ pataty andhe tamasy agnau pataṃgavat | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 7.2]
yoṣiddhiraṇyābharaṇāmbarādidravyeṣu māyāraciteṣu mūḍhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 8.1]
pralobhitātmā hy upabhogabuddhyā pataṃgavan naśyati naṣṭadṛṣṭiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 8.2]
stokaṃ stokaṃ grased grāsaṃ deho varteta yāvatā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 9.1]
gṛhān ahiṃsann ātiṣṭhed vṛttiṃ mādhukarīṃ muniḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 9.2]
aṇubhyaś ca mahadbhyaś ca śāstrebhyaḥ kuśalo naraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 10.1]
sarvataḥ sāram ādadyāt puṣpebhya iva ṣaṭpadaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 10.2]
sāyantanaṃ śvastanaṃ vā na saṃgṛhṇīta bhikṣitam | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 11.1]
pāṇipātrodarāmatro makṣikeva na saṃgrahī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 11.2]
sāyantanaṃ śvastanaṃ vā na saṃgṛhṇīta bhikṣukaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 12.1]
makṣikā iva saṃgṛhṇan saha tena vinaśyati | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 12.2]
padāpi yuvatīṃ bhikṣur na spṛśed dāravīm api | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 13.1]
spṛśan karīva badhyeta kariṇyā aṅgasaṅgataḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 13.2]
nādhigacchet striyaṃ prājñaḥ karhicin mṛtyum ātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 14.1]
balādhikaiḥ sa hanyeta gajair anyair gajo yathā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 14.2]
na deyaṃ nopabhogyaṃ ca lubdhair yad duḥkhasaṃcitam | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 15.1]
bhuṅkte tad api tac cānyo madhuhevārthavin madhu | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 15.2]
suduḥkhopārjitair vittair āśāsānāṃ gṛhāśiṣaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 16.1]
madhuhevāgrato bhuṅkte yatir vai gṛhamedhinām | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 16.2]
grāmyagītaṃ na śṛṇuyād yatir vanacaraḥ kvacit | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 17.1]
śikṣeta hariṇād baddhān mṛgayor gītamohitāt | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 17.2]
nṛtyavāditragītāni juṣan grāmyāṇi yoṣitām | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 18.1]
āsāṃ krīḍanako vaśya ṛṣyaśṛṅgo mṛgīsutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 18.2]
jihvayātipramāthinyā jano rasavimohitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 19.1]
mṛtyum ṛcchaty asadbuddhir mīnas tu baḍiśair yathā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 19.2]
indriyāṇi jayanty āśu nirāhārā manīṣiṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 20.1]
varjayitvā tu rasanaṃ tan nirannasya vardhate | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 20.2]
tāvaj jitendriyo na syād vijitānyendriyaḥ pumān | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 21.1]
na jayed rasanaṃ yāvaj jitaṃ sarvaṃ jite rase | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 21.2]
piṅgalā nāma veśyāsīd videhanagare purā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 22.1]
tasyā me śikṣitaṃ kiṃcin nibodha nṛpanandana | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 22.2]
sā svairiṇy ekadā kāntaṃ saṃketa upaneṣyatī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 23.1]
abhūt kāle bahir dvāre bibhratī rūpam uttamam | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 23.2]
mārga āgacchato vīkṣya puruṣān puruṣarṣabha | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 24.1]
tān śulkadān vittavataḥ kāntān mene 'rthakāmukī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 24.2]
āgateṣv apayāteṣu sā saṃketopajīvinī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 25.1]
apy anyo vittavān ko 'pi mām upaiṣyati bhūridaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 25.2]
evaṃ durāśayā dhvastanidrā dvāry avalambatī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 26.1]
nirgacchantī praviśatī niśīthaṃ samapadyata | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 26.2]
tasyā vittāśayā śuṣyadvaktrāyā dīnacetasaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 27.1]
nirvedaḥ paramo jajñe cintāhetuḥ sukhāvahaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 27.2]
tasyā nirviṇṇacittāyā gītaṃ śṛṇu yathā mama | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 28.1]
nirveda āśāpāśānāṃ puruṣasya yathā hy asiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 28.2]
na hy aṅgājātanirvedo dehabandhaṃ jihāsati | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 29.1]
yathā vijñānarahito manujo mamatāṃ nṛpa | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 29.2]
piṅgalovāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 30.1]
aho me mohavitatiṃ paśyatāvijitātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 30.2]
yā kāntād asataḥ kāmaṃ kāmaye yena bāliśā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 30.3]
santaṃ samīpe ramaṇaṃ ratipradaṃ vittapradaṃ nityam imaṃ vihāya | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 31.1]
akāmadaṃ duḥkhabhayādhiśokamohapradaṃ tuccham ahaṃ bhaje 'jñā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 31.2]
aho mayātmā paritāpito vṛthā sāṃketyavṛttyātivigarhyavārttayā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 32.1]
straiṇān narād yārthatṛṣo 'nuśocyāt krītena vittaṃ ratim ātmanecchatī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 32.2]
yad asthibhir nirmitavaṃśavaṃsyasthūṇaṃ tvacā romanakhaiḥ pinaddham | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 33.1]
kṣarannavadvāram agāram etad viṇmūtrapūrṇaṃ mad upaiti kānyā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 33.2]
videhānāṃ pure hy asminn aham ekaiva mūḍhadhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 34.1]
yānyam icchanty asaty asmād ātmadāt kāmam acyutāt | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 34.2]
suhṛt preṣṭhatamo nātha ātmā cāyaṃ śarīriṇām | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 35.1]
taṃ vikrīyātmanaivāhaṃ rame 'nena yathā ramā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 35.2]
kiyat priyaṃ te vyabhajan kāmā ye kāmadā narāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 36.1]
ādyantavanto bhāryāyā devā vā kālavidrutāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 36.2]
nūnaṃ me bhagavān prīto viṣṇuḥ kenāpi karmaṇā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 37.1]
nirvedo 'yaṃ durāśāyā yan me jātaḥ sukhāvahaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 37.2]
maivaṃ syur mandabhāgyāyāḥ kleśā nirvedahetavaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 38.1]
yenānubandhaṃ nirhṛtya puruṣaḥ śamam ṛcchati | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 38.2]
tenopakṛtam ādāya śirasā grāmyasaṅgatāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 39.1]
tyaktvā durāśāḥ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi tam adhīśvaram | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 39.2]
saṃtuṣṭā śraddadhaty etad yathālābhena jīvatī | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 40.1]
viharāmy amunaivāham ātmanā ramaṇena vai | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 40.2]
saṃsārakūpe patitaṃ viṣayair muṣitekṣaṇam | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 41.1]
grastaṃ kālāhinātmānaṃ ko 'nyas trātum adhīśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 41.2]
ātmaiva hy ātmano goptā nirvidyeta yadākhilāt | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 42.1]
apramatta idaṃ paśyed grastaṃ kālāhinā jagat | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 42.2]
śrībrāhmaṇa uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 43.1]
evaṃ vyavasitamatir durāśāṃ kāntatarṣajām | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 43.2]
chittvopaśamam āsthāya śayyām upaviveśa sā | [BhāgPur, 11, 8 43.3]

{BhāgPur, 11, 9}
śrībrāhmaṇa uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 1.1]
parigraho hi duḥkhāya yad yat priyatamaṃ nṝṇām | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 1.2]
anantaṃ sukham āpnoti tad vidvān yas tv akiñcanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 1.3]
sāmiṣaṃ kuraraṃ jaghnur balino 'nye nirāmiṣāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 2.1]
tadāmiṣaṃ parityajya sa sukhaṃ samavindata | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 2.2]
na me mānāpamānau sto na cintā gehaputriṇām | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 3.1]

anvaśikṣam imaṃ tasyā upadeśam ariṃdama | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 9.1]

tadaivam ātmany avaruddhacitto na veda kiṃcid bahir antaraṃ vā | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 13.1]
yatheṣukāro nṛpatiṃ vrajantam iṣau gatātmā na dadarśa pārśve | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 13.2]
ekacāry aniketaḥ syād apramatto guhāśayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 14.1]
alakṣyamāṇa ācārair munir eko 'lpabhāṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 14.2]
gṛhārambho hi duḥkhāya viphalaś cādhruvātmanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 15.1]
sarpaḥ parakṛtaṃ veśma praviśya sukham edhate | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 15.2]
eko nārāyaṇo devaḥ pūrvasṛṣṭaṃ svamāyayā | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 16.1]
saṃhṛtya kālakalayā kalpānta idam īśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 16.2]
eka evādvitīyo 'bhūd ātmādhāro 'khilāśrayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 16.3]
kālenātmānubhāvena sāmyaṃ nītāsu śaktiṣu | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 17.1]
sattvādiṣv ādipuruṣaḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 17.2]

jihvaikato 'mum apakarṣati karhi tarṣā śiśno 'nyatas tvag udaraṃ śravaṇaṃ kutaścit | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 27.1]

tais tair atuṣṭahṛdayaḥ puruṣaṃ vidhāya brahmāvalokadhiṣaṇaṃ mudam āpa devaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 28.2]
labdhvā sudurlabham idaṃ bahusambhavānte mānuṣyam arthadam anityam apīha dhīraḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 29.1]

evaṃ saṃjātavairāgyo vijñānāloka ātmani | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 30.1]
vicarāmi mahīm etāṃ muktasaṅgo 'nahaṃkṛtaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 30.2]

brahmaitad advitīyaṃ vai gīyate bahudharṣibhiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 9 31.2]

{BhāgPur, 11, 10}
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 1.1]

yo 'sau guṇair viracito deho 'yaṃ puruṣasya hi | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 10.1]

athaiṣām karmakartṝṇāṃ bhoktṝṇāṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 14.1]
nānātvam atha nityatvaṃ lokakālāgamātmanām | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 14.2]

tattadākṛtibhedena jāyate bhidyate ca dhīḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 15.2]

bahvantarāyakāmatvāt kṛṣivac cāpi niṣphalam | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 21.2]
antarāyair avihito yadi dharmaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 22.1]
tenāpi nirjitaṃ sthānaṃ yathā gacchati tac chṛṇu | [BhāgPur, 11, 10 22.2]

baddho mukta iti vyākhyā guṇato me na vastutaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 1.2]

indriyair indriyārtheṣu guṇair api guṇeṣu ca | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 9.1]

na stuvīta na nindeta kurvataḥ sādhv asādhu vā | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 15.1]

kṛpālur akṛtadrohas titikṣuḥ sarvadehinām | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 28.2]

amānī mānadaḥ kalyo maitraḥ kāruṇikaḥ kaviḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 30.2]
ājñāyaivaṃ guṇān doṣān mayādiṣṭān api svakān | [BhāgPur, 11, 11 31.1]

{BhāgPur, 11, 12}
śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 1.1]
na rodhayati māṃ yogo na sāṃkhyaṃ dharma eva ca | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 1.2]
na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo neṣṭāpūrtaṃ na dakṣiṇā | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 1.3]
vratāni yajñaś chandāṃsi tīrthāni niyamā yamāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 2.1]
yathāvarundhe satsaṅgaḥ sarvasaṅgāpaho hi mām | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 2.2]
satsaṅgena hi daiteyā yātudhānā mṛgāḥ khagāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 3.1]
gandharvāpsaraso nāgāḥ siddhāś cāraṇaguhyakāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 3.2]
vidyādharā manuṣyeṣu vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ striyo 'ntyajāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 4.1]
rajastamaḥprakṛtayas tasmiṃs tasmin yuge yuge | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 4.2]
bahavo matpadaṃ prāptās tvāṣṭrakāyādhavādayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 5.1]
vṛṣaparvā balir bāṇo mayaś cātha vibhīṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 5.2]
sugrīvo hanumān ṛkṣo gajo gṛdhro vaṇikpathaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 6.1]
vyādhaḥ kubjā vraje gopyo yajñapatnyas tathāpare | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 6.2]
te nādhītaśrutigaṇā nopāsitamahattamāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 7.1]
avratātaptatapasaḥ matsaṅgān mām upāgatāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 7.2]
kevalena hi bhāvena gopyo gāvo nagā mṛgāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 8.1]
ye 'nye mūḍhadhiyo nāgāḥ siddhā mām īyur añjasā | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 8.2]
yaṃ na yogena sāṃkhyena dānavratatapo'dhvaraiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 9.1]

vigāḍhabhāvena na me viyogatīvrādhayo 'nyaṃ dadṛśuḥ sukhāya | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 10.2]

śrīuddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 16.1]
saṃśayaḥ śṛṇvato vācaṃ tava yogeśvareśvara | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 16.2]

śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 17.1]
sa eṣa jīvo vivaraprasūtiḥ prāṇena ghoṣeṇa guhāṃ praviṣṭaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 17.2]
manomayaṃ sūkṣmam upetya rūpaṃ mātrā svaro varṇa iti sthaviṣṭhaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 17.3]
yathānalaḥ khe 'nilabandhur uṣmā balena dāruṇy adhimathyamānaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 18.1]
aṇuḥ prajāto haviṣā samedhate tathaiva me vyaktir iyaṃ hi vāṇī | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 18.2]

ayaṃ hi jīvas trivṛd abjayonir avyakta eko vayasā sa ādyaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 20.1]
viśliṣṭaśaktir bahudheva bhāti bījāni yoniṃ pratipadya yadvat | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 20.2]

ya eṣa saṃsārataruḥ purāṇaḥ karmātmakaḥ puṣpaphale prasūte | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 21.2]
dve asya bīje śatamūlas trinālaḥ pañcaskandhaḥ pañcarasaprasūtiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 22.1]
daśaikaśākho dvisuparṇanīḍas trivalkalo dviphalo 'rkaṃ praviṣṭaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 22.2]
adanti caikaṃ phalam asya gṛdhrā grāmecarā ekam araṇyavāsāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 23.1]
haṃsā ya ekaṃ bahurūpam ijyair māyāmayaṃ veda sa veda vedam | [BhāgPur, 11, 12 23.2]

{BhāgPur, 11, 14}
śrīuddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 1.1]

ātmā ca karmānuśayaṃ vidhūya madbhaktiyogena bhajaty atho mām | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 25.2]
yathā yathātmā parimṛjyate 'sau matpuṇyagāthāśravaṇābhidhānaiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 26.1]
tathā tathā paśyati vastu sūkṣmaṃ cakṣur yathaivāñjanasamprayuktam | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 26.2]

śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 32.1]

hṛtpuṇḍarīkam antaḥstham ūrdhvanālam adhomukham | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 36.1]

nūpurair vilasatpādaṃ kaustubhaprabhayā yutam | [BhāgPur, 11, 14 40.2]

paramāṇumaye cittaṃ bhūtānāṃ mayi rañjayan | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 12.1]
kālasūkṣmārthatāṃ yogī laghimānam avāpnuyāt | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 12.2]
dhārayan mayy ahaṃtattve mano vaikārike 'khilam | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 13.1]
sarvendriyāṇām ātmatvaṃ prāptiṃ prāpnoti manmanāḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 13.2]

viṣṇau tryadhīśvare cittaṃ dhārayet kālavigrahe | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 15.1]
sa īśitvam avāpnoti kṣetrajñakṣetracodanām | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 15.2]
nārāyaṇe turīyākhye bhagavacchabdaśabdite | [BhāgPur, 11, 15 16.1]

{BhāgPur, 11, 16}
śrīuddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 1.1]
tvaṃ brahma paramaṃ sākṣād anādyantam apāvṛtam | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 1.2]

śrībhagavān uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 6.1]

saṃvatsaro 'smy animiṣām ṛtūnāṃ madhumādhavau | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 27.1]

ahaṃ yugānāṃ ca kṛtaṃ dhīrāṇāṃ devalo 'sitaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 28.1]
dvaipāyano 'smi vyāsānāṃ kavīnāṃ kāvya ātmavān | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 28.2]
vāsudevo bhagavatāṃ tvaṃ tu bhāgavateṣv aham | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 29.1]
kimpuruṣānāṃ hanumān vidyādhrāṇāṃ sudarśanaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 29.2]
ratnānāṃ padmarāgo 'smi padmakośaḥ supeśasām | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 30.1]
kuśo 'smi darbhajātīnāṃ gavyam ājyaṃ haviḥṣv aham | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 30.2]
vyavasāyinām ahaṃ lakṣmīḥ kitavānāṃ chalagrahaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 31.1]
titikṣāsmi titikṣūṇāṃ sattvaṃ sattvavatām aham | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 31.2]
ojaḥ saho balavatāṃ karmāhaṃ viddhi sātvatām | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 32.1]
sātvatāṃ navamūrtīnām ādimūrtir ahaṃ parā | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 32.2]

aham etat prasaṃkhyānaṃ jñānaṃ tattvaviniścayaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 37.3]
mayeśvareṇa jīvena guṇena guṇinā vinā | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 38.1]
sarvātmanāpi sarveṇa na bhāvo vidyate kvacit | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 38.2]
saṃkhyānaṃ paramāṇūnāṃ kālena kriyate mayā | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 39.1]

vīryaṃ titikṣā vijñānaṃ yatra yatra sa me 'ṃśakaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 40.2]

manovikārā evaite yathā vācābhidhīyate | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 41.2]

yo vai vāṅmanasī samyag asaṃyacchan dhiyā yatiḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 16 43.1]

{BhāgPur, 11, 17}
śryuddhava uvāca | [BhāgPur, 11, 17 1.1]

svargiṇo 'py etam icchanti lokaṃ nirayiṇas tathā | [BhāgPur, 11, 20 12.1]
sādhakaṃ jñānabhaktibhyām ubhayaṃ tad asādhakam | [BhāgPur, 11, 20 12.2]
na naraḥ svargatiṃ kāṅkṣen nārakīṃ vā vicakṣaṇaḥ | [BhāgPur, 11, 20 13.1]
